After Power Workers' Strike, They Petitioned the Municipal Council Yesterday Afternoon

The Company Strictly Refused Workers' Entry

Party and Government Sent Personnel to Investigate the Truth

Fei Xindun Is Scheduled to Reply Tomorrow Morning

The Electrical Workers' Union Discussed How to Respond

The National News Agency reports that since the Shanghai Electric Power Company's Yangshupu New Plant dismissed three workers without cause the day before yesterday and refused to pay pension benefits, more than a thousand workers have gone on strike. The strike continued yesterday afternoon, but workers at the Feilun Road Old Plant have not yet joined. In the afternoon, since Saturday is normally a day of rest, all the workers went to the Municipal Council to petition at noon. As a result, they were promised a response tomorrow morning (Monday). The Party and Government have sent special commissioners to investigate the truth. The police have taken special precautions. The details are as follows:

Refusing Entry and Demanding Pension Benefits

Workers at the Electric Power Company's New Plant went to the plant as usual at 7:00 a.m. yesterday, but the company had secretly deployed a large number of detectives beforehand and refused to issue badges, so more than a thousand workers could not enter. The workers believed that the company was terminating the work of all the workers, so they went to the office to negotiate. At 8:30 a.m., they went to the main office of the Electric Power Company at the intersection of Jiangxi Road and Nanjing Road to demand pension benefits and put forward five people, including Zhang Changsheng, to request an audience with General Manager Elte, but they were refused. Seeing that their goal was not achieved, the workers gathered and did not disperse. The Public Concession Police had been informed in advance and, fearing trouble, dispatched a large number of Chinese and foreign detectives to monitor the scene. When the workers went to the office in a group to demand pension benefits, four of the workers came by bicycle. Due to an accidental collision with a rickshaw, the detectives there detained them in the police station under the pretext of fear of trouble. They were only released at 11:30 a.m.

Petitioning the Municipal Council En Masse

At 11:00 a.m. yesterday, about a thousand workers from the New Plant in Yangshupu set off for the Municipal Council on Sima Road, intending to petition General Manager Fei Xindun. They arrived at their destination at 12:00 noon. More than a thousand workers stood around Jiangxi Road in front of the bureau. Due to the large number of people, many workers also went to stand on the land in front of the American church opposite. Four representatives from the workers' side, Zhang Changsheng, Zhu Afu, Zhu Haosen, and Bao Defu, went inside to seek an audience with General Manager Fei Xindun. General Manager Fei, together with Counselor He Deji, personally received them. The representatives then stated that the company authorities had handled things inappropriately and dismissed workers without cause, and requested assistance to negotiate on their behalf. As a result, Fei agreed to go to the company yesterday afternoon to consult with General Manager Elte and to encourage an early solution. He also ordered the workers to maintain order and to send representatives to the bureau at 9:00 a.m. on Monday to await a reply. Thereupon the workers withdrew.

Party and Government Investigate the Truth of the Labor Dispute

Since accepting the workers' petition on the afternoon of the day before yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Headquarters dispatched Zhu Jintao from the Third Section and Dai Yongchan from the Municipal Party Headquarters to investigate the truth of the labor dispute yesterday morning. They first went to the main office at the intersection of Jiangxi Road and Nanjing Road to meet with General Manager Elte to inquire about everything. Then they went to the Fourth District Electrical Workers' Union on Tiantong Road to ask the standing committee members about the truth, so that they could make a report and the Party and Government could discuss solutions. It is heard that a mediation will be conducted on Monday.

Meeting of Group Leaders at the Old Factory Responds

The Water and Electricity Workers' Union of the Four Districts, due to the Shanghai Electric Power Company's New Factory dismissing workers and then refusing to pay pension funds, resulting in a general slowdown, is now refusing workers entry to the factory. Therefore, it is scheduled to hold a meeting of group leaders at 3:00 PM at the Tiantong Road Clubhouse to discuss countermeasures. It is heard that workers at the old factory, if the company insists on not allowing workers to enter or leave the factory, will also stage a walkout starting on Monday to support the workers and decide to collect severance pay and disband.

Company Announcement: All Dismissed

Yesterday morning, a notice was posted at the side gate of the Shanghai Electric Power Company at the intersection of Jiangxi Road and Nanjing Road. It stated, roughly, that former employees of the Yangshupu New Factory are scheduled to receive their wages on October 3rd in the factory's sign room, and they may go there to collect them at that time.

Company Report: Reasons Given

Yesterday, regarding the labor unrest, the company issued a statement in English to various newspapers explaining the reasons for this incident. After 8:00 PM on Friday, the power plant workers suddenly announced a strike without prior notice to the company for any consultation. The company was greatly shocked because the company serves society and has a heavy responsibility and is very willing to consult with its employees. However, since no requirements were heard in advance, and no workers requested contact, the company knew nothing until the workers went on strike. What is the purpose of the strike, and why did the workers resort to this tactic? The company believes that it has a great responsibility to society and workers and is deeply concerned. Therefore, it advised the workers not to rashly strike, which would endanger the lives of countless workers who rely on the electricity industry. Moreover, this strike was carried out without any procedure. The company believes that this action shows that the workers are ignorant of the facts and lack a sense of responsibility to the public, resulting in this unfortunate incident.

Capital's Side Indicates Countermeasures

Yesterday, a reporter from the Guomin News Agency, considering the importance of the power workers' strike and its impact on public safety, specifically visited Mr. Eltert, the vice president of the company, to inquire about the company's policy for dealing with the labor unrest. He was received and informed of everything in detail. According to the conversation, the company was quite surprised by the sudden strike of the workers at the new factory because the workers had not given any notice in advance, nor had they sent official representatives to discuss the matter. Therefore, the company did not know the reasons for the strike. The number of strikers today is the same as yesterday, with more than 500 workers from the new factory, all from the coppersmithing and repair departments, having no impact on power generation. As for the company's countermeasures, they are currently under negotiation and have not yet been determined. It is rumored that the company is hiring White Russian workers to replace the striking workers, which is not true. However, there were originally a small number of White Russian workers, and their number has not increased since the strike occurred.

Police Precaution: Extraordinarily Strict

The police are paying close attention to this matter. In addition to stationing a large number of armed detectives, about a hundred, at the Yangshupu New Factory, the old factory on Feilun Road has also strengthened its defenses. More than ten Chinese and Western detectives have also been dispatched to the company's office on Nanjing Road, standing guard near the front and back side doors to prevent accidents.

Today is Sunday: Workers Rest

Today is Sunday, and the company's office and its affiliated new and old factories are closed as usual. Workers do not enter the factory, so there will definitely be no development in the labor unrest today, and no accidents will occur. Tomorrow is Monday, and the result of the Municipal Council's consultation with the company will be answered. If the workers find it satisfactory, the labor unrest can be resolved. However, in case of a decisive break, the old factory may also join the slowdown to provide assistance. As for the electricity supply, the capital side claims that there is absolutely no problem.

Kaicheng Factory Requests Relief to Save Domestic Sulfuric Acid

from the Danger of Foreign Goods Dumping

Shanghai Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Co., Ltd. submitted a document to Chairman Chiang and the ministries, stating that it is a domestic sulfuric acid manufacturing factory suffering from the pressure of foreign goods dumping and is on the verge of collapse. It earnestly requests urgent relief to maintain domestic production and strengthen the national economy. The memorandum states that acid production is a basic chemical industry, just as iron production is a basic mechanical industry. If acids cannot be produced domestically, then all acid raw materials required by the chemical industry will inevitably depend on foreigners. This will not only result in a huge leakage of wealth, but if foreigners were to cut off their supply, all chemical industries, even military industries, would be destroyed. Its impact on national survival is indeed significant. With this in mind, the merchants were approved by the two ministries of military and political industry in the nineteenth year to raise funds to organize the Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Co., Ltd. After experiencing repeated incidents, we have been operating painstakingly for three years, and only this spring were we able to ship goods. According to the current equipment, 15 tons of sulfuric acid can be produced daily, about 5,000 tons per year, equivalent to about 84,000 piculs, which, according to the statistics of customs imports over the years, is sufficient to meet the needs of the whole country. However, since this spring, due to the dumping of foreign goods, the market price has plummeted from 17 taels of silver per 200-pound box to 10 taels. Since then, Japanese goods have become even more intensified and dumped on a large scale. If delivered at the Shanghai docks, the price is reduced to 7.5 yuan in Japanese gold, plus tariffs and passport fees, the total is less than half of the previous price. Under this situation, the merchant factory had no choice but to reduce production, which resulted in higher production costs and made it more difficult to compete with foreign goods. The merchants cannot bear to see this unique merchant-run sulfuric acid factory to decline. Therefore, we are compelled to report the facts and request your Excellency to examine and approve emergency relief. The relief methods are analyzed and presented to your Excellency as follows: (1) It is proposed that the government provide subsidies to relieve the urgent difficulties of the merchant factory. The governments of all countries adopt subsidy methods for industries related to national strength, subsidizing a certain amount each year to protect them. Our country's industry is in its infancy, and it wants to compete with foreign goods that have strong capital, superb technology, and political power, and non-economic dumping. If the government does not provide special subsidies, its failure is inevitable. Therefore, the merchant factory proposes that your Excellency consult with the Executive Yuan and order the Ministry of Finance to provide a subsidy of 100,000 yuan per year for two years so that the capital can be consolidated and development can be expected. (2) It is proposed that the government exempt tariffs and reduce the freight of state-run sea and land transportation agencies to reduce the burden on merchant factories. The Basic Industry Incentive Law promulgated by the government has provisions for exempting export and re-export tariffs on equipment and raw materials, and reducing the freight of state-run sea and land transportation agencies. The merchant factory has previously submitted an application to the relevant ministries in accordance with the law and has been approved to do so, but it has not yet been approved. Now that the merchant factory is facing a critical situation due to the oppression of foreign goods, it can only request your Excellency to consult with the Executive Yuan and order the relevant ministries to exempt tariffs and reduce freight so that the merchant factory can survive. (3) It is proposed that the government increase the import tax on foreign sulfuric acid to avoid the harm of dumping. In order to protect their industries, all countries have built high tariff barriers to restrict or prevent the intrusion of foreign goods. According to the statistics of the total number of sulfuric acid imports in the Republic of China in the 21st year, excluding military tax exemptions, there are about 50,000 piculs. The official tax is 5.5 jiao of customs gold per picul, which is 7.05% of the ad valorem tax. The tax rate is unparalleled. We earnestly request your Excellency to consult with the Executive Yuan and order the Ministry of Finance to specially increase the import tax on sulfuric acid, at least to 1.65 yuan of official customs gold per picul, which is sufficient to prevent the harm of dumping. (4) It is proposed that the government control the import of foreign goods, protect the domestic market, and enable domestic factories to develop independently. Controlled economy has been adopted by countries all over the world, and our country cannot be an exception. Therefore, on the one hand, the annual import quantity of sulfuric acid should be controlled by the government. Applications for import passports for foreign sulfuric acid beyond a certain quantity should be strictly rejected. At the same time, the government should strictly order educational institutions, military institutions, and even agricultural and industrial experimental farms to purchase domestic sulfuric acid. In this way, domestic goods can retain the domestic market. The above are all indispensable methods of relief. We implore your Excellency to consider the danger of national industry and promote the development of military industry, and approve its implementation. It is not only the fortune of the merchant factory, but also the future of the country and the nation will benefit from it.

Northeast General Wang Yizhe came to Shanghai from Tianjin yesterday to discuss important official matters. He did not stop in Beijing. Therefore, he sent a telegram of thanks to the various circles in Beijing who were preparing a welcome meeting. I will go to Shanghai in the next few days and will not stop in Beijing. I am ashamed and dare not accept the welcome from all circles. Please decline on my behalf first. Two Shipping Companies Request Equal Treatment for State-Run and Private Shipping Industries

Shanghai Hezhong Shipping Company and Dazhen Shipping Company sent a letter to the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association, stating: We saw in the Shen Bao on September 24th that China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Longhai Railway Bureau signed a contract for sea-land cargo intermodal transport, which will be implemented on October 1st. After reading this news, our companies were greatly frightened. Haizhou belongs to Donghai County in Jiangsu Province and is the only port of Linhong Port, and the eastern terminal of the Longhai Railway. All products from Gansu, Xinjiang, Shaanxi, Henan, and other provinces are loaded on ships there and transferred to various ports. In the past, the domestic steamships were reluctant to go forward because the area was remote and full of bandits. Only one or two foreign ships were there. The passengers and cargo of Longhai Railway were also transferred from Xuzhou to Jinpu, and then to Pukou, and then to Shanghai. Not only was the transportation procedure very difficult, but the transfer time was also extremely long, so merchants regarded it as a scourge. With this in mind, our companies resolutely pooled funds and successively established Hezhong Shipping Company and Dazhen Shipping Company, specializing in the Dapukou to Shanghai route. Hezhong Company first purchased the Haizhou, Zhengzhou, and Xuzhou steamships. Dazhen Company followed suit, measuring the waterway of Dapukou Port, building two new diesel steamships, Yongping and Yongan, and adding Yongji, sailing on a regular basis. Furthermore, because the docks and warehouses of the Longhai Railway had been in disrepair for many years, and the goods were piled up in the open air, resulting in too much loss, we also purchased land, dredged mud, and built docks and steel-concrete warehouses at the mouth of Dapukou, so that loading and unloading were convenient, and the goods were well protected. Passengers praised each other, and sea transport gradually developed. From this point alone, it is enough to prove that without the painstaking efforts of our companies, the cargo transport of the Longhai Railway would never have been so developed today. Even if it were developed today, its shipping rights would have been monopolized by foreign merchants long ago, and it may not have allowed Chinese merchants to intervene. Over the years, our companies have suffered great losses because the business on this route is light from May to September every year. The ships can only load coal to supplement their income. This year, even the small amount of coal has disappeared. However, in order to maintain the shipping line on this route, our companies still dispatch steamships as usual, even though they are losing money every day. Unlike the wild steamships, when there are prosperous months, they compete to open steamships, even more than a dozen steamships, lowering the freight and engaging in competition. By the time it is a light month, they change to other ports. Even in the case of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, although it is the earliest steamship company in our country, it has never sailed long-distance services to that port, but only occasionally dispatches one or two steamships during prosperous months to engage in competition. Moreover, the steamships dispatched are all entrusted to other companies as agents, and no branch offices are set up in that port. Think about it, our companies must maintain normal operations when there is little cargo, and we cannot exclusively occupy the advantage when there is a lot of cargo. The fact that there are more losses than profits in our business over the years can be seen generally. The reason why our companies operate painstakingly and support themselves is nothing more than to circulate inland production and prevent foreign steamships from intruding. Last year, the Ministry of Railways issued a notice to all railways to implement intermodal transport. The Longhai Railway Bureau first contacted our companies for sea-land intermodal transport, and everything was ready. Our companies were also fully prepared and waiting to implement it. Now, suddenly there is a saying that the Bureau has independently signed a intermodal transport contract with China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. If this news is true, will our companies' business not be plunged into desperation? The steamships, docks, and warehouses of our companies are specially set up for opening up the shipping line on this route, and the investment is very large. In addition, the losses over the years are not small. If the shipping of this route is exclusively contracted to China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, then what business can our companies do? Foreign steamship companies often have discounts, and the government still has subsidies. Now our authorities are actually using state-run steamship companies to exclusively handle shipping, wiping out the merchant-run shipping industry. It is not reasonable to evaluate it, and it does not seem to be a fair approach to the government's aim to protect the shipping industry. For the sake of the future of our business and the livelihood of the sailors, we have to fight for it with the Railway Bureau. If the statement that the Bureau signed a contract with China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has indeed been signed, please cancel it quickly. If it has not been signed, please stop it so that state-run and private shipping industries can jointly load and receive the same treatment, and seek development for the route. It is very much hoped. We dare to state everything together and humbly request that the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association forward it to the Railway Department and the Ministry of Communications of the Executive Yuan to sympathize with the merchants' difficulties and approve our request. We would be extremely fortunate. Respectfully to the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association, Hezhong Shipping Company, and Dazhen Shipping Company.

China National Aviation Corporation Held Annual Shareholders Meeting Yesterday

Income Gradually Increases...Losses Decrease

China National Aviation Corporation held its fourth annual shareholders meeting at the company on Guangdong Road at 3 pm yesterday. Chinese representatives present were Huang Jiangquan, Dai Enji, Wang Xianhua, and Nie Kaiyi. American representatives present were Bispei, Band, and Newlett. The managing director reported on the business situation, stating that the company's business losses for the one year from July 1, 1932, to June 30, 1933, totaled 484,933.24 yuan. The total business losses for the three years since the start of business were 1,011,157.05 yuan in the first year, 955,319.97 yuan in the second year, and 484,933.24 yuan in the third year, totaling 2,451,410.26 yuan. However, the company's revenue in the third year increased by 261,073.70 yuan compared with the previous year, and expenses were reduced by 234,285.63 yuan. The Shanghai-Beiping air route was opened on January 10 this year, with three flights per week. As of June 30, its income was only 40,099.15 yuan. During this period, the Ministry of Transportation allocated 98,500.00 yuan to the company to make up for the losses, for which the company should be grateful. In April this year, American United Airlines purchased the ownership of China Airways from Continental Airlines, and 45 percent of the company's shares are owned by China Airways. The company's aviation mileage has greatly increased due to the opening of the Shanghai-Beiping line. In the second half of the 21st year, only 215,274 miles were flown, and in the first half of the 22nd year, 288,698 miles were flown, an increase of 73,424 miles. As for the number of mail items carried, it decreased by 14.5 percent in the first half of the 22nd year due to the increase in postage, but the income increased by 14.5 percent. Although the average increase rate of postal revenue in these six months was only 14.5 percent, the postal revenue in June of this year increased by 24 percent compared with the average monthly revenue in the second half of the 21st year, which shows that although all industries are currently in decline and trade is sluggish, the company's revenue is increasing month by month. It is expected that the business will increase greatly and the expenses will be reduced after the shareholders agree to purchase faster new aircraft. The invested capital can finally be rewarded. The Claims Association Clashed with Detectives Again Yesterday

Two Women Injured

The Indemnity Association of the Disaster Area of our Ministry has twice resulted in tragedy due to claiming indemnity from insurance companies, but both have not been resolved. Unexpectedly, one wave has not subsided, and another wave has risen. At 10 am yesterday, a team of more than 200 people, led by committee members Wang Zhixiang and Ma Rugen, went to Howang Insurance Company on Guangxi Road to claim compensation. However, the insurance companies had already resolved not to recognize the compensation at the Huashang Insurance Company Association the night before, so they politely rejected the claims representatives. Since the claims members could not get what they wanted, and they thought that the instigator was the Huashang Insurance Company Association, they turned to the Huashang Insurance Company Association at No. 38 Aidoa Road to negotiate. The representatives of the association stated the reasons for not recognizing the compensation, but the claims members still insisted that the insurance companies must pay compensation. The two sides held each other for a long time. The members of the Indemnity Association were determined not to stop until they reached their goal and stayed in the association. For a time, the traffic at the gate was blocked, and onlookers gathered. Yang, the representative of the Insurance Association, seeing that the situation was not good, called the Public Concession Police at 3 pm and sent a large number of Chinese and Western detectives to the scene to carry out the expulsion. The insurance policyholders refused to disperse. The detectives repeatedly expelled them without success, so they used force to suppress them, and a small disturbance occurred. As a result, two female policyholders, Yu Jin (68 years old) and Yao Chen (37 years old), were injured and immediately sent by car to the Red Cross Branch on Xinzha Road for treatment. The rest of the people did not disperse automatically until dusk and agreed to go to Huashang to claim compensation again tomorrow. It is heard that the injuries of the two injured women are quite serious.

The Red Cross Allocated Relief Clothing to Shaanxi Province

Shaanxi Province has suffered from drought for years, and the number of disaster victims is increasing day by day. The Shanghai Chinese Red Cross recently responded to the request of General Zhu Ziqiao to appeal for the orphanage in the province and allocated 60 boxes of lined relief clothing, totaling more than 10,000 pieces. General Zhu and Yang Hucheng, the Director of the Pacification of the province, had agreed on the transportation method in advance. The Beijing Office of the Shaanxi Pacification Commissioner's Office has sent personnel to contact the Red Cross and requested the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to transport the relief clothing to Beijing free of charge and hand it over to the Beijing Office of the Shaanxi Pacification Commissioner's Office, which will then be responsible for the westward transportation.

The Southern Sichuan Chongbao Qiwu County Flood Relief Association was Established

Elected Chairman and Vice Chairman and Various Staff Members

Borrowed 300,000 Yuan from Chinese Banks to Release Relief

The Shanghai Pudong Southern Sichuan Typhoon and Great Flood Relief Association and the Chongbao Qiwu County Flood Relief Association held a joint meeting at the Renji Shantang on Yunnan Road at 5 pm yesterday. More than 70 representatives from both sides were present and jointly elected Du Yuesheng as the temporary chairman to discuss and decide on the name of the Jiangsu Southern Sichuan Chongbao Qiwu County Flood Relief Association. The details are recorded as follows:

List of Attendees

The attendees yesterday included Xu Shiying (Huang Bode's proxy), Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Wen Lanting, Huang Bode, Li Zicai, Huang Renzhi, Gui Yanfang, Zhang Xiaoliang, Zhu Shaoqi, Yuan Ludeng, Jin Hongxiang, Zhao Jinqing, Pang Jingzhou, Jin Tingsun, Mu Ouchu, Qin Runqing, Fei Gongxia, Qu Shaoyi, Shi Liangcai, Zhu Zhu, Xu Jishuang, Jin Houcheng, Sun Xiangshu, Qian Jingping, Ma Boshen, and others, totaling more than 70 people.

Resolutions

After performing the etiquette, the chairman reported, and then the discussion began. (1) The chairman proposed that based on the request of the Chongbao Qiwu County Flood Relief Association, the Southern Sichuan Relief Association and the Chongbao Qiwu County Relief Association should be merged and a new name should be determined. (Resolution) The two associations should be merged and renamed (Jiangsu Southern Sichuan Chongbao Qiwu County Flood Relief Association. (2) The election of the chairman and vice chairman. (Resolution) Du Yuesheng was elected as the chairman of the association. As for the vice chairman, in addition to the original three vice chairmen of the Southern Sichuan Association, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yiting, and Huang Zhu, Wang Dankui and Zhang Gongquan were elected as vice chairmen. (3) Raising funds will take time, but the disaster area is in urgent need of relief. How should a resolution be made? (Resolution) First, borrow 200,000 yuan from the Bank of China and 50,000 yuan each from the Pudong and Zhonghui Banks to release emergency relief. At the same time, each representative will be responsible for soliciting donations from all parties to repay the bank's advance. (4) The appointment of representatives to be responsible for contacting the bank and guaranteeing the loan. (Resolution) Yang Zixiong, Gui Yanfang, and Jin Houcheng were appointed as representatives to contact the bank for the loan. Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Huang Hanzhi, Gui Yanfang, Shi Liangcai, Wang Dankui, Jin Houcheng, Zhang Gongquan, Jin Tingsun, and other ten people were appointed as loan guarantors. (5) Who should collect the donations raised by the association on behalf of the president? (Resolution) In addition to the originally designated Zhonghui and Pudong Banks, the Bank of China will also be entrusted to collect the association's donations. (6) The appointment of representatives to inspect and investigate the disaster area. (Resolution) Xu Jijiang, Jiang Qian Ting, and Fan Kaitai were appointed as inspectors and investigators of the disaster area. (7) Each county appoints one representative to the general office. (Resolution) Zhang Bochun from Chuansha, Shen Zijian from Nanhui, Lu Caifu from Chongming, Jin Houcheng from Baoshan, and Gu Nanqun from Qidong were appointed, and Vice Chairman Huang Hanzhi was appointed to be stationed in the association to take charge of everything. (8) The location of the association's office. (Resolution) The Renji Hall was borrowed as the association's office. (9) How are the responsible staff members of the county branches generated? (Resolution) They will be appointed by the respective counties, and the list will be submitted to the association for safekeeping to become skilled workers. (10) The organization of the branches. (Resolution) The organization of each branch is the same as that of the general association. The rest are omitted. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Haimen Fellow Villagers Gather to Discuss Disaster Relief

Haimen County, outside Wusongkou, suffered from hurricanes and heavy rain on the 9th and 10th of September. Although requests have been made to the Commissioner's Office and the County Government for urgent relief, nothing concrete has been expressed to date. The people from the county in Shanghai were anxious when they heard about it, so they convened a meeting at the Haimen Disaster Relief Support Association on Youri, with more than 70 representatives including Yu Qingyu attending. Lu Chongpeng, Yang Tianan, and Yu Jingzi were elected as the presidium. After the etiquette, Lu Chongpeng reported on the disaster situation, and it was resolved that (1) a telegram should be sent to the superiors to reduce taxes and allocate relief; (2) a letter should be sent to charitable organizations such as the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Association and the Chinese Jisheng Society to quickly send personnel to allocate funds for emergency relief; (3) a letter should be sent to Haimen County to send personnel to the association to petition various agencies in Beijing Province; (4) each member should do their best to solicit donations from all walks of life; (5) committee members should be elected, including Lu Chongpeng, Zhu Nianzu, Yang Tianan, Xu Xiaolong, Shen Yaocheng, Cao Liangqiao, Lu Tingtao, Yang Zhili, Lu Xusheng, Yu Jingyu, Shen Zitong, Wang Qinfang, Yang Songpu, Jin Jinkang, Fei Xingfa, Yu Qingzhou, Fan Qifu, and Chen Rong as executive committee members, and Mao Zuquan, Yu Zhendong, Chen Fu, Shi Baixiu, Ji Mingyou, Shen Xibin, Huang Qiesheng, Jiang Tingfang, and Fan Fayuan as supervisory committee members; (6) Lu Chongpeng was elected as chairman, and Yu Qingyu and Yang Tianan as vice chairmen. Zhu Nianzu, Yang Songpu, Wang Qinfang, Yu Qingzhou, Jin Jinkang, Chen Rong, and others were elected as standing committee members; (7) Lu Chongpeng was elected as general affairs, Xu Xiaolong as fundraising, Yang Songpu as cashier, and Chen Xusheng as statistics. The charter was approved.

Detailed Report on the Severity of the Henan Disaster Received by the Jiseihui Society

The China Jiseihui Society recently received a report from the Henan Disaster Relief Association in Beijing, stating that Henan province is unfortunately plagued by war and natural disasters every year. The people are displaced, and their hearts are weary. This year began with drought, followed by severe locust plagues, and recently, the Yellow River surged suddenly, with the water level rising more than ten feet higher than usual. It carried mud and sand, rushing forward fiercely. Once it overflowed, due to the breach of the Changyuan levee in Huaxian County, the water poured into the area, submerging up to four hundred villages and causing losses of thirty million. The entire county was turned into a watery realm, with no crops remaining. The water from the Yellow River in Yucheng County entered from the border of Cao County, surging and vast, reaching depths of over ten feet and widths of over two miles. Farmlands and houses were almost entirely washed away, with incalculable damage. In Wenxian County, the river rose, and the dikes overflowed, causing floods that spread over ten miles. Homeless victims were scattered everywhere. Other areas such as Lingbao, Shaanxi, Mianchi, Mengjin, Xin'an, Gongxian, Wuzhi, Sishui, Lanfeng, Minquan, Kaocheng, Shangqiu, Fengqiu, Guangwu, Zhengxian, Zhongmu, Kaifeng, Chenliu, Anyang, Linzhang, Mengxian, Kangwu, Jiyuan, and Qinyang Counties also suffered severe damage due to the Yellow River overflowing. It is estimated that over two thousand villages and towns have been affected. In some county towns, the floodwaters surged suddenly, destroying documents. In other areas, entire villages were washed away, leaving no trace. The disaster is extremely severe, unprecedented in history. Helpless people are everywhere, with no hope of a harvest. The dead are gone, while the living, either supporting the elderly and carrying the young, perch atop roofs, or, having lost their children and spouses, cling to trees alone. The sound of weeping fills the wilderness, a scene too horrible to bear. This is a historical catastrophe and a rare human tragedy. Those who see it are horrified, and those who hear of it are heartbroken. However, the disaster area is too vast, and there are too many victims. All shelters and relief supplies are insufficient without massive funds. It is difficult to provide effective relief. A cup of water to put out a cartload of burning firewood is truly futile. Soon autumn will end, and winter will arrive, bringing fierce winds and heavy snow. Lacking both clothing and food, how can they survive? Thinking of the future is chilling. It is hoped that the entire nation will show compassion, use drawings of displaced people, and appeal for help, extensively providing relief to save these survivors. They will be grateful for the immense kindness. The report indicates the disaster is extremely serious, affecting nearly thirty counties, with those suffering less severely not even included. These dozens of counties are already like hell on earth. They seek death but cannot find it and cry to heaven but receive no response, with no way out. Alas, it is a tragedy. Though we appeal to various charitable organizations, how can they have such great power to provide relief? Fellow countrymen at home and abroad, quickly take off your clothes and share your food, saving these disaster-stricken people who are barely alive and cannot survive long. Though their voices are hoarse from crying, they still cling to a final breath, waiting to be saved.

Lu Swastika Society Prepares for Winter Relief

The Shanghai Office of the Southeast General Headquarters of the World Red Swastika Society received a letter from the Jinan Red Swastika Society, reporting on the detailed plans for preparing winter relief. We are now excerpting it as follows: "Esteemed Sirs, due to the recent floods in Shandong Province, our society, as is its duty, dispatched teams to provide rescue. The Swastika General Headquarters and the Yantai and Qingdao branches also sent eight teams to Shandong to provide relief. The Wuxi-Changzhou Swastika Society also continued to provide emergency relief. The Shanghai Red Swastika Society also sent teams to Shandong to provide rescue. In total, various parties have raised funds of approximately 170,000 to 180,000 yuan. Government relief has also released hundreds of thousands of yuan. However, the emergency relief period has now passed, and hundreds of thousands of victims in over ten counties are exposed to the elements. With the sharp autumn winds, how can they endure? Moreover, winter is approaching, and it is necessary to prepare cotton clothing and establish soup kitchens to truly save people. Our society has telegraphed various parties to discuss winter relief. We plan to raise 100,000 yuan to start the winter clothing and soup kitchen projects so that hundreds of thousands of victims will not die of cold and hunger. We are enclosing over ten photos of the disaster area, showing victims naked, exposed to the elements, or in a sea of water. The tragic situation is heartbreaking to hear and painful to see."

Mr. Danbo of Japan Conserves by Reducing Expenses to Donate to Disaster Relief

Donating Three Thousand Yuan Accumulated Over the Years

Sent Yesterday to the Charity Relief Association for Distribution

A person claiming to be Mr. Danbo of Japan came to the Renji Hall Charity Relief Association yesterday afternoon with three thousand yuan in banknotes and a note, saying that he wanted the money to be used for disaster relief to help the victims. The association staff asked for his current address to send a thank-you letter, but he firmly refused to disclose it. The association issued a receipt, and he left. People like Mr. Danbo are truly admirable. The note is transcribed below: "The Yellow River breach has affected six provinces, and millions of victims are suffering. I have a compassionate heart but lack the power to help. Now, I am donating three thousand yuan, saved over the years by reducing expenses, to be used for disaster relief in the six provinces. I ask that the esteemed gentlemen distributing the funds carefully consider how to allocate the money practically and without wasting it. I trust this is done. Sincerely, Mr. Danbo."

New Japanese Embassy Military Attaché Suzuki Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

According to the local "Shanghai Mainichi Shimbun," the newly appointed Japanese Embassy Military Attaché, Lieutenant General Suzuki Mitsuharu, arrived in Shanghai at 10:00 AM on the 30th with his wife, Chiyoko, and daughter, Kazuko, aboard the Japanese mail ship "Takita Maru." Many Japanese officials went to the pier to greet him. He previously served in Shanghai around 1916-1917 and is very familiar with the local situation. Later, he was transferred to Manchuria and was a key figure in the invasion of our three eastern provinces during the Mukden Incident.

British and French Detectives Jointly Ambush Robbers at Luzon Road, Killing One

Yuanji Draft Bank Received Payment

Four Robbers Broke In and Stole Everything

-Three Robbers Escaped, One Killed, Stray Bullet Hits Passerby-

Mr. Zhuang, a Ningbo native, lives at 35 Fuming Village, Foch Road, in the Public Concession. He is in the financial business. He set up the Yuanji Draft Bank in a spare room inside his residence, hiring Qiu Songlin as the manager. Mr. Zhuang only managed the overall planning, and traveled by car. He became a target for criminals. Yesterday was the end of the month for settling accounts, and the Mid-Autumn Festival was approaching, so the bank sent staff to collect payments from various places, receiving over one thousand yuan in cash. Suddenly, four robbers arrived, two dressed in short jackets and two in long gowns. One robber acted as a lookout, while the others entered the house from the back door and broke into the bank's accounting room. They brandished guns, ordering everyone to be silent. They then stole the over one thousand yuan in cash and fled through the back door. Mr. Xu Lansheng, Mr. Zhuang's chauffeur, was about to enter the house when he saw the situation and knew something was wrong. He immediately turned back and followed closely, seeing three robbers fleeing towards the wasteland to the west. The other robber was trying to hire a rickshaw to escape. Upon seeing this, Mr. Xu bravely rushed forward and shouted, "Catch the robbers!" The robber panicked and told the rickshaw puller to turn into the alley next to the Jiuxing Cinema, intending to flee into the French Concession. Unexpectedly, French Constable No. 386 was patrolling the area and saw the pursuit. He ordered the rickshaw to stop. The robber, in desperation, pulled out his gun and opened fire on the constable. The French constable returned fire. At the same time, Public Concession Constable No. 3031 and Tanshui Road Constable No. 1441 heard the alarm and arrived to help. A fierce firefight ensued. Although the robber was wounded, he continued to flee until he reached Luzon Road, where he collapsed and died on the spot. The constable reported to the Xinzha Police Station, and the body was sent to the Renji Hospital. It was found that he had been shot seven times, all in vital areas. The body was then transferred to the coroner's office for examination. During the firefight, a passerby named Zhang Miaotou was grazed in the left foot by a stray bullet. He went to the Renji Hospital for treatment and was discharged. The other robbers are currently being pursued by the Public Concession and French Concession police.

When Well-Fed, Lin Yaoxuan Falls for a "Fairy Jump"

The Hospital Director's Wife is Alluring

A Foreign Goods Broker Introduces the Couple

A Large Man Breaks in, Displaying a Fierce Demeanor

Coerced into Signing an IOU in the French Concession

-Three People Arrested After Reporting to the Police-

Lin Yaoxuan, a Sichuan native, 28 years old, travels between Sichuan and Shanghai, trading in silver ear and foreign goods. He resides in Shanghai at No. 37, Yiji Sichuan Gang Zihao, Huicheng Lane, 46 Route Tenant de Vaux, in the French Concession. He has accumulated some savings. Recently, being alone in Shanghai, he could not avoid the boredom of sleeping alone. He was looking for a companion to relieve his loneliness. A few days ago, a familiar foreign goods broker, Hu Ruiting, a Zhenjiang native (30 years old, residing at No. 11 Yong'an Lane, Rue Père Robert), introduced a young woman, Shen Wu, to Lin, claiming she was the wife of Shen Shoukang, the director of Jiankang Hospital at 25 Avenue Joffre. (Note: Shen Shoukang is a broker for the Kangye Tobacco Company. He accumulated wealth and founded a hospital, but he is not a doctor and hires doctors to provide treatment.) Lin found her beautiful and, after talking with her, found her gentle and quite charming. Seeing that his plan was succeeding, Hu asked Lin to go to a hotel with her. Lin agreed. At 2:00 PM, Hu accompanied Lin and Shen Wu to Room 523 on the fifth floor of the Central Hotel on Wuma Road. Hu then pretended to go to the restroom and slipped away. Seeing that Hu had left, Lin closed the door, and he and Shen Wu became more intimate, expressing their love for each other. Suddenly, three large men pushed open the door. One of them claimed to be Shen Wu's husband, slapped Lin and Shen Wu, and accused Lin of seducing his wife. While they were arguing, two more men arrived, beating Lin severely and threatening to take him to the police station. Lin had no choice but to beg them for mercy. The five men then began to negotiate, demanding that Lin pay 1,000 yuan in compensation. Since Lin had no cash, they first seized the gold watch he was wearing and 15 yuan in cash. After arguing until after 3:00 PM, the five men took Lin to the Law Office of Zhang Wei at No. 5, across from the Second District Court on Route Chevalier Garnier in the French Concession. (Zhang was out, so they drafted a contract, forcing Lin to write two IOUs for 500 yuan each, totaling 1,000 yuan, with Chen Yi as the guarantor, due on October 1st (today), but writing the date of the IOU as July 14th. After signing the IOUs, they released Lin. At this point, Lin knew he had been scammed. The First Police Station refused to accept his report. He reported to the French Concession police, saying he had been kidnapped and escaped, requesting an investigation. Director Jin Jiulin and Deputy Inspector Jiang Changwen of the Special Service then questioned Lin about his kidnapping, realizing he had been scammed, falsely imprisoned, threatened, and extorted. That night, they led detectives Dai Rongji and Geng Quanchang to arrest Hu Ruiting. Hu confessed to the involvement of Chen Fuliang (the guarantor on the IOU), a Hangzhou native, and Li and Hong Erren, from Zhuji, who lived at No. 3 Yongshun Lane, Xujiahui Road, at the end of Caishi Road. The detectives rushed to the location at 9:00 AM yesterday, but Chen and Li had already left. They searched the residence, recovering the stolen gold watch and two IOUs. After waiting for about half an hour, Chen and Li returned and were arrested. They then went to arrest Shen Shoukang and Shen Wu, but the couple had already fled. Chen, Li, and Hu were taken back to the police station and sent to the Criminal Court of the Second District Court, where Judge Zhang Chaozu tried the case. Police lawyer Yuan Jiahuan stated that the police had not yet completed the investigation and that accomplices were still at large, requesting that the defendants be detained temporarily and the trial postponed for a week to apprehend the remaining suspects. Lin Yaoxuan then testified about the scam. Chen Fuliang testified that he was 32 years old, formerly served in the military, and was friends with Shen Shoukang. Yesterday, Shen called him to say his wife had been abducted and asked him to help find her at the Central Hotel. The plaintiff begged Shen to pay the damages, so he suggested they go to a law office to write a document. Hu Ruiting testified that Lu Xinghao introduced him to Shen Wu, and he introduced her to Lin Yaoxuan for adultery. They had already booked a room three times, and he knew nothing about the extortion. Li Hong testified that he was 30 years old, came to Shanghai on the 28th, worked at Jiankang Hospital, and stayed at Chen Fuliang's residence. Shen Shoukang invited him to go with him that day, but he was not present for the rest of the events. After reviewing the testimony, the court ordered a retrial on October 6th, and the defendants were remanded to custody.

Social Telegraphs to be Implemented Today

Specially Designed Envelopes to Cater to Social Psychology

The Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications will begin implementing social telegrams today, such as those for New Year's greetings, congratulations, and condolences. The cost is four cents per word for telegrams sent to other provinces and two cents per word for telegrams sent within the province, with a minimum of twenty words. If a telegram is less than twenty words, it will be charged as twenty words. The telegram fee is one-fifth cheaper than usual. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency interviewed Mr. Hua Shijian, the business director of the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, who said that after the implementation of social telegrams, it will be implemented nationwide. The Ministry of Communications will improve social telegrams to cater to the psychology of social figures, such as using red envelopes for New Year's and congratulatory telegrams and plain-colored envelopes for condolence telegrams.

The Issue of Restoring Shanghai South Public Buses

Since the Shanghai South Public Bus Company ceased operations due to poor management, public buses in the Shanghai South area have not been restored, causing great inconvenience to citizens. Recently, a merchant applied to raise funds to operate the buses, but the Public Utilities Bureau, mindful of past failures of commercial operations, fears repeating the same mistakes and affecting public transportation. Therefore, it plans to operate the buses itself and is actively planning and applying to the Municipal Government for approval. Once approved, it can proceed with the operation. The rumor that the Public Utilities Bureau plans to transfer the operation to the Xingye Trust Company contradicts the organizational law and the organizational rules of the Shanghai Municipal Government and is not true.

A New Masterpiece on Military Science (Essentials of Warfare)

Mr. Yang Jie, the president of the Army University, previously wrote the book "Essential Reading on National Military Affairs" in the autumn of last year, which was praised by military scholars. This spring, while resisting the Japanese army in Huairou, he wrote "Essentials of Warfare," which discusses modern military situations and tactics in detail, paying particular attention to the latest inventions in new weapons. This could only be done by someone with extensive knowledge and experience. The book is divided into two parts, totaling over 100,000 words. The first part focuses on theory, divided into nine chapters, detailing the meaning of war, the causes of war, the reasons why war cannot be eliminated, the essential elements of warfare, the future trends of war, the preparation for modern war, and strategy, tactics, and command authority. The second part focuses on weapons, divided into five chapters, detailing the latest weapons, such as physical weapons, chemical weapons, artistic weapons, germ weapons, and subterranean warfare weapons. Each is illustrated, making it easy to understand.

The German Haikyo Bo Grand Circus Arrives in Shanghai Soon

The world-renowned Haikyo Bo Grand Circus will arrive in Shanghai next Tuesday. The entire troupe and animals will arrive on a chartered ship from Duisburg. The grand opening is scheduled for 9:15 AM on Saturday, October 7th. There will be two performances daily, with an additional performance on Sundays. The address is the former site of the Gezhi Road Liu Hua Hotel. This is the first time the Haikyo Bo Circus has performed in the Far East. They are bringing many rare animals, including a very ferocious two-horned rhinoceros, which is under special guard to prevent injuries. Other animals include bears of various colors (white, black, and brown), African and Korean leopards, elephants, Arabian dromedaries, horses of various sizes and colors, chirping deer, and kangaroos. In addition, there are many rare birds. With so many animals, the circus owner had to spend a fortune to charter a ship for transportation. Upon arrival in Shanghai, the animals will be unloaded at the Hongkou Wharf. The ship also carries the world-renowned performers, including acrobats who perform incredible aerial stunts, riders on galloping horses, and other amazing performers. The son of the circus owner, Haikyo Bo, has also come with the troupe. He is the most famous person in the troupe. For the enjoyment of the Shanghai people, the troupe will begin performing various amazing techniques every day from 10:00 AM. Admission is only fifty cents for adults and twenty cents for children. The Haikyo Bo Circus has been famous for a long time and will provide satisfaction to those who pay the price. It is particularly admirable that they pay attention to the comfort of the audience's seating. There will be no interruptions during the performance. During the performance period, there will be large buses traveling to and from the circus to transport spectators for their convenience.

New Regulations for Customs Clearance of Tugboats and Barges

Navigation Administration Certificate Accepted in Lieu of Ministry of Transportation License

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Bo Lede, Customs Commissioner, issued Public Notice No. 1320 yesterday, which stated: Regarding the scheduled implementation of the tugboat and barge acceptance regulations, as mentioned in this Customs' Public Notice No. 1318, we now follow government orders: (1) Starting December 1st of this year, tugboats and barges applying for a license from the Ministry of Transportation can use the tugboat and barge inspection certificate issued by the Navigation Administration in lieu of the license for customs clearance until the license is obtained. The procedure is the same as when a ship uses a registration certificate in lieu of a license for customs clearance. (2) The validity period of this tugboat and barge inspection certificate for customs clearance is set at three months, calculated from the date of issuance of the certificate. All shipping merchants should be aware of this. This notice is hereby issued.

Strongman Deng Guifang's Performance at the Jingwu Hall Yesterday

Five Amazing Skills

New National Art Record

The War Zone Refugee Relief Association, for the sake of relieving refugees, invited overseas Chinese strongman Deng Guifang to perform his skills yesterday afternoon at 2 PM at the central auditorium of the Jingwu Athletic Association on Beisichuan Road, near the Yokohama Bridge. More than 500 people attended, with Yan Zhifang and Chu Huiseng presiding. The details obtained are recorded below:

Historical Report

Among the attendees were Chu Huiseng, Yan Zhifang, Feng Shaoshan, Zhao Ruikang, and over 500 others. Yan Zhifang presided and reported that strongman Deng Guifang was from Guangdong. Since childhood, he admired the Shaolin Temple martial arts and went there on foot to practice internal and external boxing. Feeling it was not enough, he went to Hong Kong for further study, also finding Western techniques had unique points. He practiced for several years and reached a state of mastery. Taking advantage of his visit to Shanghai, he was persuaded to stay for a few days to appeal for help for the disaster victims. Mr. Deng generously agreed, so a trial performance was arranged in the auditorium. If there are any errors, he welcomes guidance from the participants.

Skill Categories

After Mr. Yan's report, Deng Guifang went on stage to demonstrate his skills with deft movements. His art truly set a new national record. The skills demonstrated are as follows: (1) Bending a six-inch-long copper nail with his teeth and then breaking it with his hands. (2) Bending a square iron into the shape of a horseshoe with his head. (3) Hammering a six-inch-long copper nail into a wooden board with his hand. (4) Bending iron into shape with his teeth. (5) Rolling iron into a double bend with his hands. (6) Bending iron with his hands and then restoring it to its original shape. (7) Using Danqi (internal energy) to allow someone to jump on his stomach from a high place. (8) Supporting himself on the ground with his hands and feet while supporting a heavy board on his shoulders and knees, with four musicians playing on top. (9) Using his body as a bridge, with a heavy board placed on him, and ten people standing on top. (10) Lifting a heavy iron hammer of about 400 pounds with both hands. (11) Holding two ropes encircled by copper rings with both hands, able to withstand the force of fifteen people. (12) Surrounding his head with a one-and-a-half-inch thick stone, totaling five inches in thickness, and shattering it with a hammer. (13) Lying naked on stones with a large stone weighing over 100 kilograms on his chest. (14) Lying naked on a bed of nails, with a thick board weighing over 400 pounds on his chest, and four musicians playing on top of the board. (15) Allowing a car to drive over his body. Other feats like the Roman iron ring and passing through rings of fire could not be performed due to lack of space.

The number of days detained before the final judgment will be deducted from the sentence at a rate of two days per day. After the sentencing, the defendant was transferred to prison (as there is no female detention center) to await the expiration of the appeal period before serving the sentence.

Outline for Railway and Highway Intermodal Transport

Eleven Articles Drafted

Order to Railway Bureau to Comply

Regarding the intermodal transport of railways and highways, the 16th National Intermodal Transport Conference has decided on an outline of eleven articles. The Ministry of Railways has issued a special order to the two railway administration bureaus to comply with them. The intermodal transport outline is transcribed below: (1) For the convenience of transportation, railways and highways may handle passenger and freight intermodal transport. (2) Intermodal transport matters include passengers, luggage, parcels, and cargo. The implementation procedures shall be negotiated and determined by both the railway and highway authorities based on the circumstances. (3) Any highway wishing to handle intermodal transport with the railway must meet the following requirements: (A) The highway bureau or automobile company must be operated by the provincial government or established with approval in accordance with the regulations. (B) The entire highway must be repaired and leveled, and bridges, culverts, and stone paving must be completed. There must be fixed employees who regularly maintain the road to prevent rain and snow from hindering traffic and delaying intermodal transport. (C) Highways transporting passengers must have clean covered vehicles. If open vehicles are used to transport intermodal luggage or parcels, they must have good tarpaulins to cover them. Their transportation capacity must meet the needs of intermodal transport so that there is no shortage of vehicles. (D) The highway must have considerable equipment that the railway deems will not hinder intermodal transport. (4) Railway and highway intermodal transport stations shall be determined by both parties. (5) The intermodal transport price shall be based on the sum of the railway and highway transport prices in principle. In special circumstances, both parties may submit separate applications for reduction, or if either party's transport price changes, the other party should be notified a sufficient period in advance. (6) Railway and highway transport fees should be collected at one time in principle. (7) The method for transferring and guaranteeing the transport fees collected by the railway and highway shall be negotiated by both parties. (8) Highways handling intermodal transport with the railway shall not handle intermodal transport with connecting waterways if it interferes with the railway's business. (9) Intermodal transport contracts shall be negotiated by both the railway and highway authorities and submitted for approval before implementation. (10) Railway and highway intermodal transport shall be based on the principle of not interfering with other railway business. (11) Intermodal transport between highways and railways regarding the acceptance and transport of luggage, parcels, and cargo, and all other matters, shall be handled in accordance with the railway regulations to the extent possible.

Sixty-Seventh Time

The sixty-seventh inspection report of the Shanghai Branch of the China Bank Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states: The members of this committee, and the appointed accountant, in accordance with the rules of this committee, inspected the special vault for issuance and inter-branch use of banknotes at the Shanghai Branch of the China Bank on September 24th, 1932. The inspection was conducted for the sixty-seventh time, and the Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance joined the inspection. The Glass Industry Association held its seventh preparatory meeting yesterday, chaired by Chen Jianting. The following important matters were decided: (1) It was decided that the general meeting of members' representatives would be held on October 15th. (2) It was decided that the general meeting would be held at the City Chamber of Commerce in Tianhou Palace. (3) Cai Renchu, Chen Jianyan, and Wang Songyuan were nominated as the presidium. (4) Wang Songyuan and Chai Wenjing were asked to draft industry regulations for review. Other matters were omitted.

News from the Introduction Department of the Global Students' Association

News from the Introduction Department of the Global Chinese Students' Association at 191 Kade Road: The association will hold a meeting for registered personnel at 10 AM today, presided over by the general secretary of the association, Mr. Zhu Shaoping. According to the association, there are currently over 1,000 registered members, with over 500 in Shanghai alone. Applicants should be college graduates with teaching experience. Those interested can contact the introduction department of the association.

Autopsy of a Girl Burned to Death

The firewood shop opened by Bian Jingen, a native of Jiangyin, at No. 42 Sanyi Lane, Yangshupu Road, suddenly caught fire in the back building around 4 PM the day before yesterday. The fire quickly spread to the front building. At that time, only Bian's five-year-old daughter, named Fengying, was sleeping in the room, so there was no time to rescue her. She was severely burned. Fortunately, the fire brigade was notified early and arrived quickly to put out the fire, so it was extinguished in just over ten minutes. The child was taken to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment, but she died soon after. The Yangshupu police ordered Detective Ji Xiucheng to investigate, and the body was taken to the autopsy center on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo of the First Special District Court visited the center to examine the body. According to Bian Jingen, 46 years old, he was not at home that day. The back building was occupied by his daughter-in-law, who was working in the factory and had not yet returned home. Therefore, he did not know the cause of the fire. His daughter was sleeping downstairs, and by the time her mother tried to rescue her, it was too late, and she was burned to death. Mr. Guo, after hearing the testimony, determined that the deceased, Bian Fengying, had indeed been burned to death before death, and the body was released to her father, Bian Jingen, to be coffined and buried with a written guarantee.

Publishing News

Science Pictorial, Upper Issue for October. Science Pictorial is a semi-monthly publication sponsored by the Science Society of China and distributed by the China Science Company at 649 Avenue Foch in this city. Its content emphasizes both images and text. Each issue, in addition to publishing new inventions in the scientific community, explains various scientific principles in simple language, introduces practical agricultural and industrial skills, and offers everyday scientific knowledge for families. It is not only loved by adults but is also a valuable resource for middle and elementary school science education. This issue features more than twenty articles, full of highlights. In the area of illustrated science, for example, the article "King Cobra" describes in detail the characteristics of snakes in various parts of China and how to recognize venomous and non-venomous snakes, while the article "The Intelligence of Monkeys" details various interesting experiments. Other articles such as "What are Fossils?" and "Plant Sprinklers" are all highly educational. In the area of national defense, there are articles on "Submarines," "Steam-Powered Airplanes," "New Trench Diggers," and "Reflective Concealment Barriers." In the area of crafts, there are articles such as "The Method of Sugar Production" and "Understanding Steel." In the area of new inventions, articles such as "Light Miles" are eagerly anticipated. There are also serial long articles such as "Illustrated Explanation of Physiology and Anatomy" and "Popular Research," which are more substantial. Short pieces such as "Air Pressure Experiment," "Soap Propeller," and "Lemon Battery," numbering dozens, are perfect for elementary school science materials. In terms of printing, it is also excellent. Each issue sells for only 20 cents, and a full year of 24 issues, including postage, costs $4.80.

Literary Bestseller: The "Literature" monthly magazine, published by the Life Bookstore, has been popular at home and abroad since its inception on July 1st due to its rich content, novel subject matter, and low price, gaining momentum every day. The inaugural issue is currently in its fourth edition, the second issue is in its third edition, and the third issue has also been reprinted. The fourth issue is published today and contains more than thirty articles, including "Daughter's Heart" by Luo Huasheng, "Tiny God" by Lao She, "Under the Roof" by Lu Yan, "Fifty Dollars" by Wang Tongzhao, "Counterattack" by Zhang Tianyi, "Sophie's Diary, Part 2" by Ling Shuhua, and "The Evolution of Journey to the West" by Zheng Zhenduo. The pictorial illustrations include twenty-one portraits of several writers who contributed to this issue, and four woodcuts by world-renowned artists, which are even more stunning than before. The retail price is 30 cents per copy, and a one-year subscription for twelve issues is $3.50 domestically and $5.90 abroad. Postage stamps are accepted at face value. Qinghe Magazine Volume 2 Starts Special Offer: The first volume, issue twenty-two of Qinghe Magazine, compiled by Mr. Chen Xiaoyi, was published on October 1st. After two more issues, it will be completed. Volume 2 has begun at a special price, with extra preferential treatment for full-term subscribers. Twenty-four issues per year, including postage, cost only $5.60. New subscribers pay $6.00 including postage. In addition to the "Annotations of Jia Ye Tang's Collection of Books," "Autobiographical Chronicle of Kesai," "Diary of Kesai," ("Wen Yi Ge Notes," "Shu Ting Zai Bi," "San Yuan Jing She Wen Cun," "Qing Shi Shuo Xin Yu," "Gu Tong Sui Bi," "Infant Postscripts," "Notes of Zhu Yizun," "Bai Zui Jian Hua," "Kuang Lu Notes," "Random Notes from the Slender Shakyamuni Room," "Tea Xiang Zhai Tan Wang," and the "Poems of Cheng Xianghai Tang Guanyongquan," "Postscripts of Zhi An Books," and dozens of other manuscripts, there will also be the unpublished manuscripts of Dahe Shanren, all related to works on bronze and stone inscriptions, calligraphy, painting, and anecdotes. In addition to the Complete Works of Xiangqilou, unpublished manuscripts include "Qi Wenduan's Diary of a Mission to Longyou" by Qi Junzao, "Notes of Scholar-Official Wen Tingshi," "Miscellaneous Notes from Shen Nanye's Bianjia Pavilion," "The Words and Poems of Bi Zhai," "Casual Talks from Liang Zhangju's Zhiyuan Pavilion," "Literary Records from Yuan Siliang's Gangfa Yizhai," "Literary Manuscripts from Li Guosong's Feidun Studio," "Poetry and Prose Manuscripts from Ge Tingjiu Zhai," "Poetry and Prose Manuscripts from Xia Jingguan's Yue An," "Parallel Prose Manuscripts from Gong An," as well as poetry, travelogues, and humorous essays by other recent individuals, totaling as many as fifty or sixty types, all of which will be published in Volume 2 as much as possible. Those who have read Volume 1 must continue reading Volume 2. After reading both volumes, it is as if you have obtained dozens of complete books. It is also heard that Volume 1 has been concluded, and the famous works will be compiled and printed in series and sold at a low price.

Published in Moscow, Berlin, Rome: The books published by the Hecheng Bookstore at 47 Ningbo Road in Shanghai have always been welcomed by readers. Now, the books "Moscow," "Berlin," and "Rome" have been published. These books are written by Yūsuke Tsurumi from Japan and translated by Tiran Jun. The content details the actual situations in Moscow under socialism, Berlin under fascism, and Rome. The characters, thoughts, national characteristics, and living situations of representatives of each country are deeply depicted. Among them, the prediction of the future of international politics is a special feature of this book. It also includes many steel engravings. The price is 60 cents per book, with postage of 11 cents. All major bookstores in this city and other places sell them.

Qianqiu Semimonthly: The ninth issue of Qianqiu Semimonthly, published by Qianqiu Publishing House at 276 Kunshan Road, has been published on schedule. In addition to the original content, Qianyun Jiang Dongliang's cartoons and comic talks, and a full page of Qianqiu comics have been newly added, which are exceptionally sharp and concise. The price is still only 10 cents per copy, 2 yuan per year, and postage stamps are accepted. Modern Bookstore on the Fourth Avenue is the general distributor, and major newsstands sell them.

"The Social and Economic History of France": This "Social and Economic History of France" is written by the French economic historian Sayon, and the original book is about 600 pages. It narrates the entire history of France from prehistory to the Great War of 1914 in detail. The content is substantial, the system is well-organized, and it is his recent comprehensive research work. It has now been carefully translated by Mr. Lu Kanru and published by Renjiang Bookstore. The translation is smooth, the intention is clear, and when there are translated words, the original text is mostly noted. Not only is it the most valuable reference book for those who study French social and economic history, but it is also an extremely important book for those who study general political economy, especially those who study Chinese social and economic history. The translated version is divided into two volumes, and the first volume has now been published. The price is 80 cents per volume. The Shenbao Service Department and major bookstores across the country sell them.

Wanglai: The third issue of the popular Wanglai Semimonthly has been published. The main items include "Review and Prospect of Shanghai Central District" by Lishan, "The Content and Burden of Chinese Fu" by Long Ding, "The Exploration of International Economic Relations" translated by Jun Chang, and "Rose Season" by Wenyi Yiqi. In addition, there are communications such as "Written at Will: Tales of Xianju" and "The Current Situation of New Guangxi." There are also multiple articles such as Wanglai Tan and Officialdom Records. The materials are novel and the writing is smooth. The price is 4 cents per issue, and the subscription fee for the whole year is 65 cents. The publishing house is at 13 Dunhe Lane, Ladu Road. The Guoguang News Agency in Suzhou and various bookstores and newsstands in this city sell them.

His treatment is unique and decisive, and patients can be cured in a short time. Those who suffer from weak joints and difficulty in having children, after his diagnosis, will all be able to achieve success, and their sufferings will disappear. In the afternoon, he provides free medical care at the Xijin Guild Hall on Haining Road, without charging medical fees.

Yu Qingfang Establishes an Obstetrics Hospital: Ms. Yu Qingfang, a German obstetrician expert, has successively served as the director of obstetrics at the Sino-German Hospital, Sino-German Obstetrics Hospital, and Shanghai Civilian Obstetrics Hospital in this city. Later, she established her own clinic at Shanhai Pass Road and Avenue Edward VII, etc., and has won the trust of society. Now, because of the development of her clinic, she has specially opened the Qingfang Obstetrics Hospital in a Western-style house at No. 2 at the intersection of Julai Road and Beidi Road to meet the needs of maternity families. The hospital officially opened yesterday, and the telephone number is 84402.

Chaozhou Heji Hospital Holds a Fundraising Variety Show: The Chaozhou Heji Hospital in this city has achieved great success since its establishment. It is now planning to expand its organization and build new hospital buildings. It is scheduled to hold a fundraising variety show at the Golden Theater on October 5th, 6th, and 7th for three days. On October 5th, day and night, the latest and most popular domestic film "Flowers of Freedom" donated by the Star Film Company will be shown, as well as the most exciting foreign sound films donated by the two philanthropists Gao Yonglian and Gao Yongjie. On the 6th and 7th, day and night, the most famous Chaozhou opera troupe, Lao San Zheng Shunxiang Troupe, will perform gratuitously. After this donation performance, the troupe will return to Chaozhou. This will be their last two days of performance in Shanghai. All ticket income will be used for the Heji Hospital Fund. The Chaozhou Fellow Association is currently jointly preparing with the hospital and many charitable philanthropists. People from both Chinese and foreign countries are welcome to visit. There will definitely be a lively atmosphere at that time.

The History and Ironclad Proof of Artificial Blood: The Wuzhou Pharmacy began selling artificial blood during the late Qing Dynasty. For more than twenty years, it has been sold throughout China, the South Seas Islands, Taiwan, the Americas, and Canada. It has been around for a long time, and its reputation has grown. This agent was originally a prescription from a British Royal physician, and the company has refined it according to the prescription. It has been presented to the Ministry of Health of the National Government and tested by official offices in various places, proving that artificial blood is indeed a pure and delicious blood tonic, with the functions of nourishing and strengthening, without any adverse side effects. It is suitable for men, women, old, and young. Since the company launched this agent, it has received dozens or hundreds of letters of thanks from consumers every day. Although the number is small, it has created a new record in tonics. During this autumn tonic season, those who suffer from neurasthenia and all deficiency symptoms can recover their health after taking "artificial blood," and its effect is magical.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather is overcast and rainy. A low pressure system has formed in the Yangtze River basin and is moving towards the coast. A hurricane has apparently approached Luzon and is rapidly advancing to the northwest-west. The weather is bad in the northern part of the China Sea. Its center, at around 4:00 PM, was within 120 miles of the intersection of 17 degrees north latitude and 120 degrees east longitude. The wind force is unknown. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 80.4, and the lowest was 59.5. On the same day last year, the highest was 85.3, and the lowest was 59.0.
