Miscellaneous News from the National Games

Urgent Request for Rosters (Nanjing, 30th) The National Games Organizing Committee urgently telegraphed the four units of Ping, Hong Kong, Yunnan, and Fujian to submit their athlete rosters by the 30th, requesting them to register via telegram.

Group Visits The committee sent a letter to various organizations and schools, stating that due to the large number of spectators expected during the Double Tenth Festival, overcrowding would be unavoidable. Groups intending to visit were required to notify the reception section of the organizing committee with their visiting time and number of people before October 8th, in order to reserve seats.

Group Exercises The elementary schools of Jing City and Pukou rehearsed Tai Chi exercises at Xingzhongmen Elementary School on the afternoon of the 30th. 191 students from the Four Academies participated, still under the direction of Chu Minyi. Xingzhongmen Elementary School was the most organized. Overall, based on the six days of district rehearsals, the performances from the Central and Eastern Districts were considered superior.

Teacher Tea Party The committee scheduled a tea party for physical education teachers from various elementary schools in Jing City at the Lizhi Society on the afternoon of October 2nd at 2 p.m. In addition, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Director and the Shaanxi Province Director Fu were sent to participate in the opening ceremony. Prizes Received Song Zheyuan of Harbin sent a letter designating Ge Dingyuan, director of the 29th Army's Beijing office, to represent him at the National Games opening ceremony, and donated one hundred yuan for prizes. Chen Bulei, director of the Zhejiang Education Department, sent a four-panel screen painting of West Lake scenery as a prize for the National Games.

Shaanxi Not Participating The National Games Organizing Committee received a telegram from Shaanxi Province stating that due to the impact of natural disasters in the province, they would not be sending athletes to participate at this time. They have telegraphed Director Fu, stationed in Beijing, to attend the ceremony.

Position of Secretary-General The position of section chief of the National Games Organizing Committee was originally held by Wu Bangwei. However, Wu was unable to attend due to his involvement in the Jiangsu Provincial Games. After repeatedly declining the position to the committee, the organizing committee decided to ask Secretary-General Zhang Xinfu to concurrently serve as section chief. However, Zhang, citing a busy schedule, found it difficult to manage both roles. As a result, Zhang, in a personal capacity, invited Wu Bangwei to Beijing to handle the allocation. Wu only stayed in Beijing for two days and then hastily departed for Zhenjiang on the 28th to take on the role of guiding the Jiangsu athletes. Therefore, the various allocations were not fully completed, and the allocation is practically inseparable from the records. The scoring sheets need to be prepared according to the allocation procedure. Therefore, Zhang Zhongfan, the section chief of the records section, had to take on the task of allocation in order to fulfill his duty of recording, which was an unavoidable situation. In recent days, Mr. Zhang has been working diligently through the night. Everyone in the committee knows this. Last night, Zhang Xinfu went to Hangzhou. Regarding Zhang's duties as Secretary-General during his absence from Beijing, someone will naturally be responsible for presiding over them, and not Zhang Zhongfan acting temporarily. Lest there be any misunderstanding, the truth is clarified as above.

Organizing Committee Appoints Additional Presidents

In addition to the appointed President of the National Games, Wang Shijie, Honorary President Lin Sen, and Honorary Vice Presidents Wang Zhaoming and Chiang Kai-shek, the Organizing Committee appointed a large number of additional Vice Presidents and Honorary Vice Presidents on the 30th as follows:

Wang Wenzheng Wins the Municipal Men's Singles Tennis Championship

3-1 Victory over Yu Tianguang

Women's Singles Belongs to Mao Yuwen

2-0 Victory over Wang Dale

The results of yesterday's finals for the municipal men's and women's singles tennis championships are as follows: Wang Wenzheng won the men's championship, defeating Yu Tianguang 3-1; Mao Yuwen won the women's championship, winning 2-0 against Wang Dale. Today's doubles matches have been postponed due to the conflict with the Lawn Tennis Club's Open Doubles Final. The finals date will be around Wednesday afternoon, still at the China Sports Association tennis courts on Hart Road. The progress of yesterday's men's and women's finals is described below:

Wang Wenzheng Defeats Yu Tianguang 3-1

Yu Tianguang's victory over Wang Wenzheng was overwhelming in the first set, winning 6-2. Who knew that he would collapse afterwards and be unable to recover? The championship was then decided. The scores are as follows:

Two to Six

Six to Zero

Wang Wenzheng Six to Three Yu Tianguang

Six to Four

Yu Tianguang's Rise and Fall The great change in the overall result could not be predicted from the momentum of the first set. Yu Tianguang served first, hitting both left and right with great advantage. His hitting technique was excellent and his errors were few. Wang Wenzheng had no way to handle this. Unexpectedly, Yu Tianguang's power was but a flash in the pan. The first serve was won by Wang Wenzheng. Yu also broke back. Yu then served again. His shot was powerful. As the ball left his hand, he rushed forward to the net for a volley. Wang Wenzheng could only watch helplessly, making it 2-1. Wang served again, strongly and deeply into both corners, making it 2-2. Yu did not falter slightly, fighting more and more bravely. Wang Wenzheng had not yet gotten his grip. The ball was always two or three inches outside the line. Thus, one game after another, Wang Wenzheng lost four games in a row. Yu Tianguang won the first set 6-2. However, his early momentum faded, and he lost three sets in a row, which was also unexpected.

Wang Wenzheng's Momentum The Yu Tianguang in the first set completely changed in the second set, becoming weak and listless. His balls went out of bounds repeatedly, or into the net. The skillful net volleys of the first set were also gone. Wang Wenzheng again and again won six games in a row, returning a blank set, which was unexpected. Each switched to a new ball, hoping Yu Tianguang would perk up, but that hope was lost. Yu served powerfully and with preparation, hitting well and winning the first game. Because Wang was out of bounds, he won another game. His momentum was sufficient. The situation changed again. He made many mistakes, and his power also greatly decreased. Wang Wenzheng took advantage of this and attacked fiercely, winning five games in a row, and winning the third set 6-3, taking the lead with two sets to one. The last set was the end of the line. Although Yu was still ahead 2-1, Wang Wenzheng took the next three games, making it a 4-2 advantage. Yu won back two games to even the score 4-4, but it was to no avail. Wang Wenzheng finished the game with 6-4. Wang Wenzheng's shots were stable, and his mistakes were few, so he deserved to win.

Mao Yuwen Defeats Wang Dale 2-0

In the women's final, Mao Yuwen won both sets against Wang Dale to win the match. The scores are as follows:

Six to Two

Mao Yuwen Wang Dale

Six to One

Wang was no match for Mao. Mao was stable and skilled, with good forehand and backhand shots, deep and far. In the first set, Mao won three games in a row. Wang won one game, then it became 4-2. Mao finished the first set with 6-2. The second set was even worse. Wang only won one game, the third game. The score finished 6-1.

No Matches Today There are no matches today due to the impact of the Open Doubles. The matches will have to rest for one day. Yu Zhizhong of the Nanjing Amateur Tennis Club has come to Shanghai and has agreed to let the Shanghai team practice at the Amateur Tennis Club's courts during the National Games, which is very kind. The results of the first week of the men's doubles are appended below:

(1) Mao Hongfa and Liang Guanying defeated Hu Qichang and Hu Qichao 9-7, 0-6, 6-2.

First Battle of the Chi Ling Chi Cup: Donghua Defeats Western Police

1-1 Draw in the Morning

Donghua Wins 2-1 in the End

The first battle of this year's Chi Ling Chi Cup between Donghua and Western Police was held yesterday at the baseball field. The weather was clear and the spectators were extremely enthusiastic. The stands were packed with people, creating an extremely lively atmosphere. To put it lightly, there were at least 10,000 spectators. As a result of 90 minutes of fighting, Donghua won 2-1.

Kuir Gives the Award for Past Achievements The Chi Ling Chi Cup began last year. Donghua won both games and won the cup. The award ceremony was delayed. Yesterday, the second year of the competition began. Before the battle, Mr. Kuir, the football director of the Western Police, held the dazzling silver cup in front of the players of both teams, made a sincere speech, and personally presented the silver cup to Lu Zhong'en, the captain of Donghua. Lu replied with a thank you. The first year's history ended, and the whistle for the second year's battle was heard in the field again.

Donghua's Power Remains the Same Donghua's performance was as good as last year. The small movements of the forwards' feet were clever and worth watching. The wings contributed a lot. The shooting in the middle was a pity. The three veterans on the middle defense line were good at assisting, but their strength was not sufficient. Perhaps they were not in the best condition. Li Ning was quite good, and Guan Xun'an made significant progress. This is something that Donghua can be pleased about. Zhou Xianyan was not yet skilled in training, so Lu Zhongs came in instead. Lu was also qualified. His crouching save of a bottom ball near the end of the game was highly praised.

Plattley's Good Skills The Western Police veteran Gash Parker Turner was not present, so it is easy to imagine what their strength was. The mainstay relied only on Plattley's goalkeeper. He had a great reputation before Zhou Xianyan, but had been out of action for several years due to injury. Now he is playing the old tune again, with the same old power. He is tall and strong, shrewd and experienced, and cannot be underestimated. The inside defense had no special features. Herre, in the middle defense line, served his duty. Weiss U was average. The forwards and the middle line were sometimes separated. Center forward Willy had no one to assist him and had no place to use his skills. Defly was okay. Jack was disappointing. The wings were frustrating.

Smiling Faces Heard Sighs The Western Police kicked off and immediately entered Donghua's feet. Li Yichen kicked the ball to the right, and Cao Qiuting rushed into the field. The spectators were energized and saw Western Police in danger. It was passed again and again, nearing the abdomen. As Li Yichen was about to set up his banner, he mistakenly touched his arm and was penalized. In the blink of an eye, it came again. Chen Jiaqiu swept the ball out behind the enemy. Wan Xianghua and Li Yichen chased forward. The inner court was empty. In the nick of time, Gibson chased to stop the advance. If Xiao Wan had shot earlier, the result might have been different. Two good opportunities were lost with the autumn wind. Unexpected danger suddenly arose on the left of the court. As Lu, the goalkeeper, was blocking left and right, he drew cheers from the audience. Because the kick-off was weak, and Feng Yunyou's assistance failed, he was tackled by the enemy. With a kick from Willy, Donghua was the first to concede. The spectators' smiling faces had not yet disappeared, and sighs came first.

Yichen's Header Makes it a Draw Donghua was angered by this blow. The five generals attacked separately. Feng Wu Tu coordinated in the middle. Li and Guan stationed troops in Guanzhong, providing assistance from afar. Western Police was greatly frightened by the growing momentum. Weiss and were helpless. Herre and Fralas looked at each other in dismay. Fortunately, the inner defense was still able to fight. Coming in and out repeatedly, Western Police was in dire straits and unable to find a way out. However, with the goalkeeper's health, it was not easy for Donghua to find a flaw. Time flew by, and in the blink of an eye, forty minutes had passed. Feng Yunyou kicked a ball to the left. Wan Xianghua went deep, passing it to the middle. Li Yichen headed the ball head-on, flying into the net. The first half ended in a 1-1 draw.

Hongguang Calmly Performs Great Feat Switching sides to fight again, they reorganized their forces. Donghua's momentum was so great that Western Police shrank back. Chen Jiaqiu, with Cao Qiuting's help, first shot, but was not accurate. Cao continued to advance, seeing that Chen Hongguang was unguarded, and took the opportunity to pass it to him. Chen, facing the empty goal, calmly and unhurriedly entered the palace. After Donghua took a 2-1 lead, the Western Police were like a plate of loose sand, open to attack. If Plattley's hands and feet had not been stable and his eyes had not been sharp, how could there have been such a slight difference in the result? Towards the end of the game, Western Police made a final struggle, taking advantage of the people's tiredness and invading the city in separate ways. For a time, the city was full of wind and rain, and every bush and tree seemed like an enemy. Willy attacked Lu's lower road in the crowd. Lu was able to catch it out by lying down. Both offense and defense were masterpieces. The battle time ended from there. Donghua won 2-1. The referee was Shen Huichun.

Anti-Drug Essay Contest

Also Open to University and Middle School Students

Ministry of Education to Determine Essay Topics

Awards for the Top Participants

Nanjing, 30th) The Ministry of Education has decided to hold an anti-drug essay contest to promote the anti-drug cause. Students from all schools can participate. On the 30th, the Ministry ordered all departments to notify the students. A copy of the contest rules is attached, outlining: (1) Each university and middle school is limited to three participants. The deadline for registration is November 15th. (2) Each university essay should not exceed 6,000 words, and each middle school essay should not exceed 4,000 words. The deadline for submitting the essays is December 15th. (3) The essay topics are: For universities: "The Actual Effects of the Local Opium Disaster and Effective Plans for Eradication." For middle schools: "The Fate of Opium Addicts." (4) Ten winners will be selected from universities and thirty winners will be selected from middle schools. (5) The winners of the contest will be awarded cash prizes, silver medals, and certificates. The top three winners from universities and the top five winners from middle schools will receive additional scholarships.

Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Educational Society Holds Member Meeting

Discussion on Individual-Centered and National-Centered Education Issues

Nomination of the Next Meeting Location and Convener

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Educational Society held its fourth member meeting at the YMCA building on Eight Immortals Bridge at 7 p.m. the night before last, to discuss individual-centered and national-centered education issues, as well as various association affairs. The details are recorded as follows:

Members in Attendance: A total of several dozen people, including Chen XuanShan, Zhuang ZeXuan, Chen HeQin, Zheng XiGu, Dong RenJian, Liao MaoRu, Xie XunChu, Tai ShuangQiu, Zhang ZhongHuan, Zha LiangZhao, Mao YanWen, Ma ZongRong, Lu KeMei, Zhang ShuYi, Ni WenYa, and Sun KangZeng. Xie XunChu was the chairman, and Zhang ZhongHuan was the recorder. A. Report Items: The chairman reported on (1) changing the meeting convocation method, and (2) in addition to the regular meeting today, welcoming Mr. Zhuang ZeXuan. Zhuang ZeXuan reported on (1) the progress of the Guangdong Branch, (2) the educational situation in Guangdong, and (3) the planned activities of the Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center.

Discussion Issues: B. Discussion Issues: (1) Xie XunChu raised the issue of individual-centered education versus national-centered education, stating that there are two issues in education: one is the purpose, and the other is the method. Individual-centered education is the method of education, and national-centered education is the purpose of education. Because the nation and the individual cannot be separated, education is to nationalize the individual, so individual-centered education and national-centered education do not conflict. (2) Zheng XiGu stated that past education has been more focused on the development of the individual and less on the consciousness of the nation. Future education should focus on cultivating the spirit of the nation. (3) Liao MaoRu stated that although past education emphasized loyalty to the monarch and love for the country, it often focused on honoring ancestors and becoming famous, thus neglecting the nation and focusing on the individual. Future education should transform the concept of the nation, and to achieve this goal, more attention should be paid to broad education. (4) Zhang YouSan stated that in reality, the government treats individual-centered education and national-centered education as opposing terms. Mr. Hu Hanmin emphasized public character and not individuality. The actions of our people are scattered, but their thoughts are not free at all. However, an excellent nation must be organized by excellent individuals. The so-called excellent individual is by no means blindly following but truly free, so individual-centered education is by no means selfishness. (5) Chen KeMei stated that both individual-centered education and national-centered education are the purpose of education and are conflicting, but the conflict between the two is relative rather than absolute, meaning that it should be decided whether to focus on the national aspect or the individual aspect according to the needs of the times. (6) Tai ShuangQiu stated that there are three starting points for education: one is the individual, two is the nation, and three is society, so it is not only individual-centered education and national-centered education. (7) Zhuang ZeXuan stated that Chinese education is centered on the nation and not on the individual, the nation, or society.

Meeting Resolutions: (1) The case of the location, time, and convener for the next meeting was resolved. It was decided that the next meeting would be convened by Ou HuaiAn, Tai ShuangQiu, Ni WenYa, and Ma ZongRong, the location would be in the Great China New Village, the issues for discussion would be determined by the convener, and the date would be set in mid-October. (2) The case of recommending representatives to contact Mr. Cai Yuanpei and Li Shizeng was resolved to be discussed at the next meeting. The meeting was adjourned.

Page 21

Spring and Autumn

Escape

— Qing

Individuals, regardless of their status, when they have been deeply involved in the world, even if they are wielding power and authority, seemingly invincible. Little do they realize that this state of affairs cannot be enjoyed for long. If you! Look at it with a true perspective, alas! It is truly like white clouds and grey dogs, changing in an instant, or like sparks from flint and flashes of lightning, impossible to grasp even a bit. To speak of more recent examples, since the overthrow of the Qing Dynasty and the establishment of the Republic of China, Sichuan's Wang RenWen and Jiangsu's Cheng XueLou were both influential figures of their time, holding military power in their hands, and certainly not insignificant lower officials. Yet, in the end, they would suddenly realize the truth, go to practice asceticism, become monks. Furthermore, Lu WeiXiang was not without a minor reputation in the diplomatic world. He did not return from abroad for a long time, and later in Europe, he entered a monastery to end his life. Thus, it can be seen that worldly fame and wealth can ultimately be shed, unlike life, which cannot be abandoned. Understanding this point thoroughly can make one realize that those who are fighting for power and profit in the dark are truly pitiable!

Now, it is heard that Sun ChuanFang, through the introduction of the Panchen Lama, has received ordination before the lamas and has also taken Xi Yue, a monk, as his teacher in Peiping. From then on, he chants sutras, worships Buddha, and becomes a disciple of the empty gate. Isn't this a strange thing? Sun ChuanFang once served as the commander-in-chief of five provinces, and none of his subordinates, such as Meng ZhaoYue, Zhou FengQi, and Lu XiangTing, were not battle-hardened generals who secretly uttered battle cries. Alas! When they went against the trend and the soldiers refused to obey orders, they were utterly defeated. Imagine! How long ago was it that this situation was like floating dust in the air, passing in an instant? To seek his past traces is to find nothing but shadows. The ancients called it "unbearable to look back." Sun ChuanFang, at the end of his heroic road, probably felt this kind of repentance, so he saw through the vanity of the world, went forth to seek a pure and happy land to spend his remaining years. From the current era of vexing punishments, war, and the suffering of the people, an era of chaos and no governance, Sun ChuanFang still has a little clarity in his mind. "Lay down the butcher's knife" and become a Buddha on the spot is a sermon for this generation of people!

However, Sun ChuanFang's ordination to study Buddhism can be regarded as redeeming the sins of his past life. It is his own affair, not his heart for the people. What does this mean? Because the heart of a Bodhisattva is to save the world, not to be weary of it. If, after having exhausted all authority, everyone thinks that the seat of the Buddha can be used as a place to hide, then lofty retirement is not allowed, let alone entering the empty gate? How can he face all sentient beings? Therefore, although Sun ChuanFang has received ordination, his qualifications for "studying Buddhism" are still not up to par. He can only be considered "escaping Chan." Moreover, whether he can cleanse his six senses, sacrifice this turbid body, and practice asceticism and poverty, I am afraid that the restless heart will be difficult to rely on. According to his own words, this time he was ordained because he had "no master in his heart and no one to rely on." In this way, it is really out of necessity, not out of faith. Haha! If the Buddha knew this, wouldn't it be a great sin not to give him a stern reprimand?

Ma Jong and the Seizing of Manchuria

— YanQiao

Ma Jong evolved from Ma Diao, Hu Shih said this long ago. However, Ma Diao only has forty cards, from one cash to nine cash, one thousand cash to nine thousand cash, one myraid cash to nine myraid cash, besides that there is a zero card. Ma Jong has one hundred and thirty-six cards, the more there is, the more variation, so Ma Jong is popular around the world and Ma Diao is being eliminated.

Wu MeiCun had the "Ma Diao destroys the country" theory, but Yang GuangXian borrowed it as material to praise the Imperial Dynasty. Of course, one side said it was the tool to destroy the country, the other side said it was the pioneer to raise the country up. On September 18th, China was in mourning, Japan was celebrating. Heaven also joined in, giving China the second storm and giving Japan a little sunshine.

At the end of Ming Dynasty, a remaining people wrote a note in his notebook, saying "No one knows when the Leaf Game came about? When JingXi came into power, the ten people with chaotic behavior forgot about sleep and food, going from night to day, calling it Ma Diao." This situation and the Ma Jong craze in various places now are not far apart. If you went to the big hotels in Shanghai to take a look, maybe "today's people are better than ancient people."

Yang GuangXian's Ma Diao introduction says: "The color of the leaves is green, green means Qing. The win is marked with red, symbolizing today's crown. The one with the most marks is called Smooth Flag, symbolizing the year. Winning means to seize Manchu, symbolizing the Manchus winning." It is convincingly attached, I cannot not admire Mr. Yang's intelligence, and it praises the system well. Not just praise, but also a prediction, aren't they really seizing Manchu now! The Japanese seized Manchuria from the Chinese and still put on an act, placing a puppet as a shield, the Chinese certainly feel pain, and wouldn't the puppet feel sad too? I wonder if the Chinese will have the day to seize it back?

Some people say that Ma Jong was created by the remaining people of Ming, the so-called "Pure One Color" "Take Apart the Tartars" terms, all are curses towards the Qing Dynasty. I am afraid this saying came from the Ma Diao preface. With praise, there will always be curses. But I also want to say that it is a prediction, you can't make Pure One Color, you make Mess One Color, that "Fake Manchu Country," isn't that making China, Japan, and Manchu into one pot? Even until now, you can't say who the real rightful owner is.

The Cricket Jumps to the City God Temple

— ShiJiu

"The cricket cries 'Qu, qu', little treasure's heart wants it; pry open the brick, peel the 'du', it jumps, jumps to the City God Temple, the incense burner and candle holder all fall down!"

This children's song is not only harmonious in its entirety, but also sings with three sighs at the end, making it even more lingering for three days without end. According to this song, it is quite in line with the meaning of comparison and metaphor. Upon investigation, there is great truth in it. If we imitate the example of Mao Gong's preface to poetry to preface it, we can obtain the following sentences:

"It satirizes greed. People's hearts are greedy and mean, and they chase after profit and desire, and they can never be at peace."

Let's take "lottery tickets" as an example. This big "cricket" is worth hundreds of thousands of dollars; how can "little treasure," who wants to get rich, not want to get it by chance! "Prying open the brick" means that they know it is not necessarily obtainable, but they want to give it a try. "City God" is a metaphor for people who are blessed by the God of Wealth. However, "ill-gotten gains do not enrich the poor!" This "City God," after getting the first prize, attracts ruffians and kidnappers, and it is difficult to live in peace in the "temple." "The incense burner and candle holder all fall down" is an extreme expression of his unease.

Let's take the "empress" as an example. This big "cricket" can make people "turn upside down"; how can "little treasure," who suffers from lust, not want to pursue it! "Prying open the brick" means trying their best to follow closely and not let go of a single step. "City God" is a metaphor for a rival in love. However, a beautiful woman is ultimately a disaster! This "City God," although triumphant in the arena of love, makes the "temple" restless, with the broom upside down. "The incense burner and candle holder all fall down" is also an extreme expression of his unease.

By extension, wanting to be an official, wanting to collect debts, can all be viewed in this way! Therefore, if the "cricket" never stops, then "little treasure's" heart will never die; and the "City God," and the "temple" of the "City God," will never be at peace, alas!

Time Comes and Luck Comes, Yu YouQing

I often hear a saying, "When time comes and luck comes, you can eat meat out of tofu." The meaning of this saying is coming true for comrades who smoke cigarettes now. I only remember that cigarette packs could be exchanged for cigarettes, or for towels, cologne, etc. I never thought that cigarette packs now have become term deposit checks in the bank.

For example, taking Red Lion brand cigarettes as an example, ten packs are worth 10,000 yuan, almost one pack has the hope of 1,000 yuan. If you throw away a Red Lion brand cigarette pack, it is equivalent to throwing away a 1,000 yuan check. For a cigarette that costs five cents, after you smoke the cigarette, the pack is still worth 1,000 yuan. Then the value of the pack is greater than the cigarette. Spending five cents has the hope of 1,000 yuan. Please have the students calculate this price, you won't be able to get the same rate, this is a shocking matter.

After smoking other cigarettes, there are golden betel nut trees, golden tripods, and gift certificates from the three major companies, placed in front of our eyes, how envious. If your forehead shines, then when time comes and luck comes, a thunderclap out of nowhere, you can become a small rich man, this is the special right of comrades who smoke cigarettes. If you want to get rich, of course you have to step up your work, which is to increase the amount of cigarettes you smoke. If you usually smoke one pack, then you have to smoke at least three or four packs. Ten years later, parents will have to teach their children the skill of smoking. No matter where you are, it will be a world of cigarettes with smoke everywhere, I never thought that after opium was popular for a while, what followed was cigarettes? In the future, people in society who do not smoke cigarettes will either be fools or idiots, don't they want to get rich! I changed the following sentence of "When time comes and luck comes, you can eat meat out of tofu." It becomes "When time comes and luck comes, you can eat money out of cigarettes." Haha!

Four Northeast Company Commanders

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Sixteen: Bitter Feelings in the Breast, Still Offer Blessings; Busy Military Affairs, Secretly Shift Troops

Whenever young people see a bride, they cannot help but feel a sense of joy. However, when JiZhi saw the bride at this moment, it was as if a sharp pair of scissors pierced straight through his chest. As he walked this way, the old Mrs. Yang JiangShi had already seen him. Fearing that something embarrassing would happen, she rushed in front of JiZhi in a few steps and said with a smile: "Mr. Gan, how did you know? Today is the day of our daughter's engagement. We are just about to go take a photo." Although JiZhi was stunned, it only lasted for two minutes. At this time, he had already woken up. If he showed a foolish appearance in front of so many people, wouldn't that be a joke? So he forced a smile and said: "This is quite a coincidence, I actually caught up with the wedding banquet. Zhao ZiQiang had already seen him too, and rushed forward two steps to shake hands with him. JiZhi shook his hand and said: "Company Commander Zhao, I haven't thanked you yet. Thanks to your introduction, I found such a position where there is work to do and no anger to suffer. Today I came just in time, there is nothing to congratulate, I wish you a happy old age." As he said this, his eyes were already shooting towards GuiZhi's body in the distance. Although GuiZhi was standing inside the door, her eyes were also shooting like lightning onto JiZhi's body. At this time, with their eyes meeting, GuiZhi had married another person. For this frustrated lover, she could not help but feel a little ashamed, so although she was very calm, a wave of heat in her heart still rushed to her face, so she couldn't help but lower her head. Zhao ZiQiang knew a little about the past relationship between JiZhi and GuiZhi in theory. Seeing his forced smile at this time, he was also very clear in his heart, so he patted JiZhi's shoulder with his other hand and said: "When I finish this, I will find a place, let's have a drink." Children's Fun World

Two Children's Works

— Zhen

The Cricket's Struggle The giant wheel of the times is rolling on. From that gentle spring, to the hot summer, it unconsciously turned to the cool autumn, turning all year round, endlessly circulating.

Autumn is coming. The autumn of the insect world is coming. In this autumn, we always hear the cries of many insects at night, as if they are holding a big concert. Among the insects, there is a kind of cricket, they have no sense of community, but have an inferior nature of mutual killing.

Once, I saw a cricket living in a pile of grass. Another cricket walked here, looking for food. When that cricket came to rob his house, they fought. As a result of the fight, both crickets died. They are of the same kind, why fight like this and sacrifice two lives, it is really not worth it!

We humans catch them and put them in cricket jars to play with. We put two crickets in a jar and lure them to fight. They don't know the temptation of humans, and they are fooled by us, fighting. In the end, it is either injury or death. The winner still cries 'Qu, qu' to ridicule his kind. This kind of insect is extremely low in its level. But alas, China is also like this, fighting with its own people. Year after year, so our China is bullied and looked down upon by foreign countries. Now we should unite and do our best to resist foreigners, and not kill each other again.

An Interesting Memory

— Zhou Ling

Time flies like an arrow, the hot summer has passed, and the cool autumn has come again. Now, I occasionally recall an interesting thing I did one evening in the summer, and I write it down below:

As the fiery sun gradually fell from the west, the earth suddenly became somewhat dark, but after a while the moon came out sparklingly. And there were countless stars next to it, also coming out with the moon, as if they were protecting the moon. The moon and the stars drove away the darkness and emitted a bright light. And the blue color of the sky, lining the silvery-white stars, made this evening even more bright and lovely, making people feel very bright in their eyes when they saw it, and even making people feel very cool in their hearts. So at this time, many men, women and children were smiling, came out to enjoy the cool air, talking and laughing, very happy.

My family was also like this. After eating dinner, we all went to the garden to enjoy the cool air. My grandmother and parents were also enjoying the cool air under the corridor. My siblings and I sat down in the pavilion and started telling stories and jokes, very happy. And the wind was very strong here, because next to the pavilion were many tall and drooping willow trees, so it was very cool. We had just finished telling a story, took a break, and looked out at the evening scenery. As we were looking out, there were many things flying there that were bright and bright, and they turned out to be countless fireflies. I hurriedly called my brother to look. After my brother looked, he said: "Let's get fans and bottles, catch them, put them in the bottle, it's very fun." I originally liked fireflies too. After hearing my brother's words, I agreed very much, so I hurried to get the fans and bottles. We clapped very hard. After a while, the bottle was full. My siblings and I all jumped up happily. We wanted to clap again, but it was already ten o'clock, so we put away all kinds of things and walked into the room, turned off the lights, and took out the bottle. It was really beautiful! It turned out that the fireflies in the bottle seemed to have turned into many small lanterns. Because I clapped so many fireflies that night, I also had the same dream after sleeping.

Banks' Joint Reserve Committee Revises Clearing House Regulations

The Clearing House established by the Joint Reserve Committee of the Shanghai Banking Association has been actively planning since its opening on January 10th of this year, and has made considerable progress. Initially, the exchange of negotiable instruments was limited to 32 exchange banks. Later, in March, all local branches of various banks joined the exchange, with each bank acting as its own agent, totaling 57 branches. Recently, three banks, including China United Savings Bank, Kwangtung Industrial & Enterprise Bank, have applied to join as exchange banks. It is heard that the application has been approved by the association and will take effect on October 2nd. Therefore, the number of banks participating in the exchange has increased from 32 to 35 (list of exchange banks attached), with a total of over 90 banks including the branches of various banks. Reviewing the monthly exchange statistics published by the association, the daily average total exchange amount is approximately 3,000 negotiable instruments, with a value of 7-8 million. This is only a centralized settlement of a portion of the financial industry, and the results are already as described above. If more parties join the exchange, there will be even more satisfactory results. Recently, in order to enhance its effectiveness and meet the needs of silver and money businesses outside the exchange banks, the exchange has proposed expanding the scope of agency exchange. At the 9th Committee Bank Representative Conference held by the association a few days ago, this matter was discussed. It was unanimously agreed that the scope of exchange should be expanded as soon as possible, and that exchange banks should provide other banks, trust companies, and money shops with the same convenience as their branches. It was decided that the agency exchange section of the association's Negotiable Instrument Exchange Regulations should be amended to reduce the responsibilities of the agent banks while expanding the scope of agency exchange. This matter concerns the entire financial industry in Shanghai. After inquiry, the reporter has obtained the content of this amended agency exchange method, and the key points are recorded below:

(1) Scope of Agency: (A) An exchange bank may be entrusted by various banks, trust companies, or member money shops of the Shanghai Money Trade Association to act as an agent for the exchange of negotiable instruments at the Joint Reserve Committee. (B) The banks or trust companies or money shops that entrust agency exchange (hereinafter referred to as "entrusting banks") are limited to those whose head offices have been operating for more than two years.

(2) Agency Contract: The entrusting bank has the obligation to comply with the Negotiable Instrument Exchange Regulations. Before the start of the agency, a contract shall be signed with the agent bank. (3) Negotiable Instruments for Agency Exchange: (A) All negotiable instruments that can be exchanged received by the entrusting bank shall be sent to the agent bank for exchange. (B) The negotiable instruments mentioned above shall be affixed with the exchange stamp of both the entrusting bank and the agent bank in addition to the original endorsement stamp of the entrusting bank.

(4) Transfer of Agency Exchange Difference: The entrusting bank shall open a current account with the agent bank for the purpose of receiving and paying the agency exchange difference.

These amended regulations will take effect on October 1st. The agency exchange system has been in place for a long time in the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan, and has proven to be quite convenient. This is because the procedures for exchange banks to join are more difficult, unlike the agency exchange system, which is simple and easy to implement. Moreover, given the large number of banks established in various countries, if all of them were to join the exchange as members, the exchange procedures would be complicated and time-consuming, which would be difficult to arrange. Given the large number of banks, trust companies, and money shops established in Shanghai and the complexity of their habits, it would be even more difficult for the entire financial industry to participate in the exchange directly than in countries such as the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan. Therefore, the need for an agency exchange system is self-evident. Now that the association has expanded the agency method, once it is realized, it is expected that all silver and money businesses in the city will use the agency exchange method, and the convenience of centralized settlement will be achieved.

List of Exchange Banks of the Joint Reserve Committee (Attached Exchange Number)

1. Bank of China 19. Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation

Yesterday, the stock exchange was shaken by rumors reported in a certain newspaper. When the market opened in the morning, all parties were selling. Although there were buyers, the market felt fatigued and unable to rise. The bond market decreased by 0.1 to 0.35 yuan. In the second session, there was some short covering, and the market price slightly recovered by about 0.2 yuan. When the market opened in the afternoon, the above-mentioned varieties were still relatively stable. Business Sutras (44)

Wood Oil and Tung Oil

Wood oil is soft and yellowish. If it encounters a southern wind, it dissolves into a pasty state. It is extracted from the tallow tree just like tung oil. Tung oil is extracted from the kernels of the tallow tree fruit. If the skin and kernels of the tallow tree fruit are pressed together, it becomes yellow and soft wood oil. The best quality is produced in Xiushan and 　yang areas of Sichuan. Jiaxing in Zhejiang is second best, and the worst is mixed 　wood oil from Jiangxi and Hubei. Currently, its use is limited to making candles and mixing into soap production. The annual production is about 100,000 dan. The quality distinction is determined by the firmness and whiteness, or softness and yellowness, and the presence of moisture. In the deep winter, it is often packed in straw bags or 　bags, but when spring arrives, it must be repackaged in 　containers to prevent melting.

Tung oil is produced in the same regions where tallow oil is found. (The tallow oil production areas were detailed in this newspaper on August 30th.) Its greatest use is as an additive to tung oil when the price of tung oil is high, as their quality and color are similar and difficult to distinguish. The annual production is about 300,000 dan. It is a liquid, and storage containers must be oil baskets or barrels to prevent leakage.

Free Talk

Snake and Sphinx

— Xu Maoyong

When I was a child, my grandmother often told me jokes and all sorts of wonderful things. I loved listening to them, and I still remember many. One time,

she said there was a type of snake that ate people, but it had a rule. When it saw a person, it would first stand its body straight up and compare it to the person's height. If the person was not as tall as it, it would eat them; conversely, if the person was taller than it, it would fall to the ground and roll to its death. Therefore, this type of snake was most dangerous to children; however, there was a way to overcome it. That is, when its body has not yet stood straight, you quickly take a bamboo pole or other thin, long object and hold it straight up, making the top of the bamboo pole higher than the snake's head, and then the snake will admit defeat.

My little heart was greatly stimulated by this story. Later, when I went to walk in the mountains and fields, I was often apprehensive, but also very much hoping that this kind of snake would come out and challenge me. Of course, a wooden stick was always tightly clutched in my hand. However, I spent more than ten years in the countryside, and my curiosity and adventurous spirit were never satisfied.

Later, when I read 兩　Qiu Yu An's "Random Notes", I learned that the origin of this kind of snake was actually in Qiongzhou, Guangdong. I had never been to Qiongzhou, so no wonder I never encountered it. However, what was recorded in the "Random Notes" was slightly different from what my grandmother described. It was said that: "When the snake measures people, it cries: I am taller. The person should also respond: I am taller, and the snake will immediately fall and die." This made defeating it even easier, and even bamboo poles and wooden sticks would not be needed.

What this kind of snake reminded me of was the mythical sphinx of ancient Greece. This monster squatted on the road to Thebes, posed a riddle for people to guess. If they couldn't guess it, they would be eaten; if they guessed it, it would throw itself into the sea and die. Later, its riddle was finally guessed by King Oedipus, and the answer was "Man." The riddle was: "What animal walks on four legs in the morning, two legs at noon, and three legs in the evening?"

To challenge people without reason, to ask riddles without reason, to eat when victorious, although it is inevitable to be domineering, but to repay with one's life when one loses, without denial, is truly "acting directly." It is unexpected that this kind of monster is quite trustworthy.

In Chinese legends, there is also something similar to the Sphinx, found in the Classic of Mountains and Seas: "Beyond the Northwest Sea, north of the Red Water, there is Zhangwei Mountain: there is a deity with a human face and a snake body, who is red, with straight eyes and upright pupils. When he closes his eyes, it is darkness, and when he opens them, it is light... This is Zhujiuyin, also called Zhulong." Also, the commentary on the Songs of Chu says: "In the northwest of the heavens there is a dark country with no sun, where a dragon holds a candle to illuminate it." That is this thing, so this monster is a messenger of light.

After being frightened by human deceit and darkness, I very much want to be with these monsters.

Prohibiting and Self-Manufacturing

— Ru Niu

According to reports, because of the large number of imported pencils and fountain pens, some places are already prohibiting their use and switching back to writing brushes. Let's not talk about irrelevant things like airplanes and cannons not being domestic products, let's just talk about paper and pens.

We won't talk about famous people who write large characters and paint traditional Chinese paintings, let's just talk about real office workers. For these people, writing brushes are very inconvenient. An inkstone and ink can be dispensed with, and ink sticks can be used instead, but what kind of ink sticks are domestic? And according to my experience, ink sticks are not something that can be used frequently. After writing a few thousand characters, the writing brush will be glued up and unusable. If one sets up an inkstone and grinds ink, unfolds paper and wets the brush, then even in the case of students copying lecture notes, the speed will probably be reduced by a third compared to using a fountain pen. They would have to not copy, or have the teacher speak slowly, which means everyone's time is wasted by a third.

The so-called "convenience" is not laziness, it means that in the same amount of time, one can accomplish more things, which is saving time, which is making a person's limited life more effective, and which is equivalent to extending a person's life. The ancients said, "It is not the person who grinds the ink, but the ink that grinds the person," lamenting the waste of life in paper and ink, and the invention of the fountain pen is precisely to make up for this deficiency.

But its existence must be in places where time and life are precious. This is not the case in China, of course, it won't be a domestic product. China has ledgers for imports and exports, but there is still no ledger for the number of people. How much material and energy do parents spend in raising and educating a single person, and yet young men and women often come to unknown ends, and no one pays attention. A mere amount of time is of course not a problem at all. Being able to live and play with a writing brush may even be a blessing, it's hard to say.

Like us Chinese, Japan has always used writing brushes. However, in Japan, writing brushes have almost disappeared, replaced by pencils and fountain pens, and there are many calligraphy practice books that use these pens. Why? Because they are convenient and save time. But aren't they afraid of "leakage"? No, they manufacture them themselves, and even ship them to China.

When something is excellent but not a domestic product, China prohibits it, and Japan imitates and manufactures it. These are two completely different approaches.

New Autumn in an Island Nation

— Ke Ling

Impressions of Qingdao, Part One

There, there is a light blue sky, and there, there is a deep blue sea. There is a paradise opened up by the Great German Empire for our wealthy merchants, young masters, and sons of nobility!

Summer is slowly ending, autumn has arrived, and the sea breeze is cool. Those who are escaping the summer heat are awakened from their dreams like a cold moon at the window, and they feel a touch of melancholy in their hearts. It seems that summer has gone too quickly, and the seawater bath has not been fully enjoyed...

Yes, summer there is worth cherishing.

The scorching wind cannot blow onto the island; there are no people dripping with sweat. Do you love to see mountains? Laoshan is not far away; do you want to play in the water? In front of you is a stretch of calm sea. You can have everything you want: dance halls, movie theaters, coffee shops... Everything that modern city dwellers need to enjoy has been carefully prepared for you.

When you have nothing to do, take a drive in a car; the road is clean and wide, undulating and winding along the mountain's slopes. On both sides of every road are dense locust trees like umbrellas, casting a belt of shade in the sunlight. It's a pity that the locust trees don't bloom in the summer; otherwise, the fragrant wind of locust flowers would fill your embrace.

Do you want to take a walk? Seaside Park, First Park, the choice is yours. Those parks are built for groups of young ladies and gentlemen, pairs of modern men and women strolling arm in arm. It is most suitable there. People with money who are escaping the summer heat always bring a companion of the opposite sex.

After lunch, take a nap and then go to Huiquan Bathing Beach!

The bathing beach there is the best in all of China! The seawater there is not muddy yellow, it is transparent blue　slice, far away against the Mo Yun Mountain, dotted with ochre-colored reefs in the middle. The sand is soft, yellow like gold. There are extremely many people, men, women, black hair that has been soaked in water, colorful swimsuits, bodies that are curved like mermaids: rolling in the waves, lying on the beach; laughter and voices are uttered at any time. There is no ethnic distinction, no national distinction, although there are more foreign men and women there than compatriots, you will not feel any different.

It is like this, floating in the waves, lying on the beach, letting the hot summer day sneak away. When you are tired, you can walk behind the beach. There are teahouses in the sparse green trees, go in and drink a glass of beer, or a bottle of Coca-Cola made from Laoshan spring water; Western music broadcast on the radio is inviting you. The blue sky turns into a black sky, and the blue sea turns into a black sea. The lighthouse on Little Qingdao flickers in the darkness: it's late!

The trestle bridge is lively at this time.

The trestle bridge: built so neatly, like a long dyke stretching straight into the middle of the sea. The waves under the bridge always sing mysterious songs. People are on the bridge, and the wind is at sea. The men and women who are strolling show the most leisurely posture. Occasionally, two or three girls walk shoulder to shoulder and laugh, a fragrant breeze passes, and behind them, one or two young men follow, pointing and commenting, making such a long, thousand-foot FollowShot. Love, comedy! The money belongs to the father, the time belongs to oneself, who else is worthy of being in love if the young men aren't?

There, there is a light blue sky, and there, there is a deep blue sea. There is a paradise opened up by the Great German Empire for my petty wealthy merchants, young masters, and sons of nobility!

Summer there is worth cherishing. But summer is slowly ending!

Yuan Zhonglang as an Official (1)

— A Ying

After reading the four volumes of Yuan Zhonglang's letters, I found one thing quite amusing, and that is Zhonglang's career as an official. His letters, according to Jiang Jinzhi's preface to "Collection of Unbinding", are "each word and each phrase, written directly with the brush as he desired, in various exquisite ways", and these letters, some are several hundred words long, others are dozens of words long, in short, flowing out from true feelings and real situations. This description of Zhonglang is very accurate. Even in his letters about being an official, it is enough for the reader to see how innocently he describes his own psychological state at any given moment. At first, being an official made him happy; therefore, when he was appointed magistrate of Suzhou County, he was extremely pleased and hurriedly wrote a letter "to the gentlemen of the same society", saying:

I have been appointed to Wu. If Wu has a magistrate like me, then the Five Lakes will have an elder, Dongting will have a lord, the wine will have a host, the tea will have a confidant, Monk Sheng will preach the Dharma, and the stone will have an elder. I only fear that the grain officials from five hundred li away will disturb me. The path of officials binds people, I do not know what the future will hold. I am writing to let you all know." At this time, Lang was a little carried away with himself, because being an official was an ideal and illusory realm for him. "Who doesn't enjoy being an official", "When I was young, I looked forward to being an official like looking forward to being an immortal", he repeatedly said in his letters. Later, this dream came true, he became the magistrate of Wu County, and this ideal fairyland was completely shattered by this stint as an official. He said that being an official was a hard thing, a painful thing, a heartbreaking thing. He believed that "my talent and knowledge are foolish, I am ultimately a person of the forest, and charging me with the people and the community is not my duty" (Draft for Returning Home), and that "being an official can really harm my life" (To Huang Qishi), and so he resigned. In a letter to Li Benjian, he described his feelings about being an official at this time, saying:

When I was young, I looked forward to being an official as if looking forward to being an immortal, enduring frost in the morning and heat in the evening, imagining that there would be endless glory. Once I got my hands on it, the taste was actually more frugal than being a scholar. As for the hardship and humiliation, it is no less than a hundred or a thousand times more, how can one not be devastated and give up the idea? It is like an infant who cries incessantly when he sees a wax sugar figure, but once he puts it in his mouth, he is afraid of spitting it out. The taste of being an official is just like this.

This is comparable to Zhonglang's confession of being an official. He no longer wanted to be an official, turning "admiration" into "aversion", and expressing his feelings to those immortal people who were still officials. He wrote a letter to Xu Shaoqing, saying:

Who doesn't enjoy being an official, only those with the truest feelings have no choice, but even then it is tasteless. When food is tasteless, even children know to spit it out; when being an official is tasteless, but one does not know to spit it out, one will inevitably vomit along with it, until one loses both body and life, this is what I worry about day and night.

Before being an official, Zhonglang saw being an official as extremely enjoyable, but after becoming an official, he felt that it was simply human hell, and it was better to leave his position and become a free and unrestrained poet. Little did he know that it was not easy to get an official position; it was not a simple matter to resign from it. This can be seen from his letter to Zhang Youyu. He said:

Being in a troubled county is like a monkey in a cage. If you want to get out, the owner will lock you up again; if you don't want to get out, it is not in your nature. You jump east and west, 𨁝

Zhonglang's resignation was actually not an easy matter. According to his letters, he was allowed to resign after seven requests. All seven "Requests to Leave Wu" are attached to the back of the letters. In the first request, he explained his illness and that his grandmother wanted him to return to the north. He　finally, he was a person of the forest, hoping to enable him to "return to his hometown early, so that even on the day of death, it would be like the year of life." The second request was a further oath, saying that if what he said in the resignation was "a single word of deceit, may the gods strike him down." The third request was another request, saying that if he could be allowed to resign, then it would truly be "heaven is high and earth is thick, how can his gratitude be exhausted." The fourth request was somewhat indignant, saying on the one hand that if he allowed him to resign, then "his remaining life would all be a gift from the Magistrate", and on the other hand expressing his determination, saying, "I would rather flee with my head in my hands and be a deposed civilian stripped of his position than wither and die in another land and be a starving ghost without support." The fifth request went further, saying, "I respectfully pack my bags and maintain my boat, awaiting the Magistrate's orders." The sixth request was the final determination, preparing to escape, he said angrily:

I already moved my wife, children, and luggage to the front path on the eleventh of this month, and I am alone in the house, waiting for the order to come down. I did not expect it to be delayed until now, with no news at all. My heart is more and more depressed, my hopes are becoming more and more isolated, and the fire is getting hotter and hotter, and the chills and fever are recurring. At this time, I am like a fish in a cauldron, unable to live and unable to die. After thinking it over and over again, the only way to preserve my body is to escape. Does the Magistrate must make me an abandoned person who discards his seal and is stripped of his official robes?

The Passionate Child (4)

— Translated by Ge Mang and Sai Zuo Zhuying

After dinner, everyone played an old-fashioned card game, and Miss White also engaged in this old-fashioned game with her girlish charm, so the trembling Luo Zhe peeked at the cards coming out of the bag, arranged his cards, reported four　with a mischievous expression, and reported five numbers with a triumphant expression! How different this was from playing that pitiful, lifeless game with his grandmother in the yellow light of a candle. "But you see he's stealing all our money, this cheat."

He covered White's cards with a quick, fiery glance, making up for the oversights, and as a result, thanks to his help, she won completely: "This is a dowry," she said as she collected the money, "You helped me earn it, Luo Zhe, let's split it."

It was time to go home; every feast must come to an end. Luo Zhe stood up, very distraught, his throat felt like it was blocked by something, and he reached out to her. Madame Capelle looked at him and couldn't bear it, so she said: "Alright, don't hesitate, hug and kiss her, since you are so eager." She lifted the child up and placed him on the table, and the tall, twenty-something girl smiled and offered her face to him. Then, a happiness that had never been experienced before flowed through him like a ray of dawn; he closed his eyes and brought his burning lips close to her cheeks, which were softer than flowers; a congestion rising from his chest disappeared into that vermilion kiss; in that one second, he felt like he fainted. Compared to the complete bliss of this virgin first love, everything the poets say seemed pale and insignificant. Every passionate kiss he gave to others afterwards was just a bland and tasteless sensuality compared to this kiss.

Ten years later, he saw her again, by which time she was a gorgeous young woman. He thought he had forgotten her. But the memories that ten years of time could not erase slipped through his heart like a childhood wisp of smoke. He remembered again that flower-like kiss on his lips. He brushed his eyes with his hand, supporting himself forcefully, not letting himself fall... (End)

Appendix: The authors of this novel, Jean Gaument and Camille Ce, are both men of letters from the old capital of Normandy, Rouen, with university degrees. Although their fates have been harsh, and they have repeatedly lost the glory of obtaining literary prizes such as the Goncourt and Balzac by a difference of one or two votes, their works are actually very worthy of reading. When they first published short stories, they won the sympathy of readers because of their artistic sincerity and their beautiful emotions, sharp and delicate observations.

Their works are often full of the charm of the homeland that makes people yearn for, depicting the lives of provincials, and in many places, they can be compared to Balzac; but compared to Balzac, there is more lovely gentleness and melancholy.

Both of them are now only around fifty years old, which, in the eyes of Westerners, means that they still have a great future.
